FOREWORD 


Here  it  is  -  the  Cook  Book  you  have 
been  waiting  for  -  More  Mortarboard 

Menus.  • 

So  many  requests  for  the  first  Mortar- 
board  Menus  came  in  after  the  supply 
was  exhausted  that  we  were  persuaded 
to  try  another  one  -  So  we  sent  out 
requests  far  and  wide  for  favorite  re- 
cipes and  have  now  compiled  the  results 

We  have  printed  them  as  "favorites," 
not  necessarily  originals. 


The  proceeds,  over  and  above  expenses, 
are  our  contribution  to  the  Sweet  Briar 
Development  Fund  -  our  special  thanks 
go  to  the  Development  Office  which  is 
backing  the  undertaking. 


^&v&v><x§es- 


Champagne  Punch 

2  cups  orange  juice 

1  cup  sugar 

2  bottles  Sauterne 

3  bottles  Champagne 

Combine  the  orange  juice,  sugar,  Sauterne 
and  chill  for  at  least  one  hour.   Just  be 
fore  serving  add  the  Champagne  which  has 
been  chilled . 

Dee  Newman 


Hot  Spiced  Cider 


1  gallon  cider 
1  stick  cinnamon 
12  cloves 


(4" 


^  teaspoon  cinnamon  powder 
^  teaspoon  allspice 


Let  stand  from  %  to  1  hour  in  large 
kettle.   Then  bring  it  to  a  boil.   Be 
careful  not  to  boil  it.   Serves  16. 


Laura  Buckham 


Instant  Russian  Tea 

18' oz .  jar  of  Tang 

lh    cups  sugar 

3/4  cup  instant  tea 

1  package  instant  lemonade  (Wyler) 

^  teaspoon  ground  cloves 

1  teaspoon  ground  cinnamon 

Mix  thoroughly.   For  each  cup  of  tea, 
use  one  or  two  teaspoons  of  tea  and 
very  hot  water. 


Maxine  Garner 


Spiced  Ice  Tea 

1  lemon  cut  in  sections 
%"  cinnamon  stick 
Pinch  coriander 

h    cup  sugar 
lh    cups  water 
5  bags  of  tea 
4  cups  cold  water 

Let  the  bags  of  tea  stand  in  the  cold  water 
overnight.  Place  the  lemon,  cinnamon,  cori- 
ander, sugar  and  water  in  a  saucepan  and 
bring  to  a  boil.  Boil  two  minutes.  Cool  and 
strain.  Remove  the  bags  from  the  tea,  pour 
in  a  jug,  add  the  lemon  liquid,  and  chill 
till  ready  to  use.  Fill  tall  glasses  with 
ice.  Fill  with  ^  gingerale,  h    tea.  Decorate 
with  mint  sprig  and  lemon  slice. 

Spiced  Tea,  Russian  Style 

20  level  teaspoons  tea 
3  pints  boiling  water 

2  cups  sugar 
1  cup  water 
Juice  of  10  lemons 
Handful  crushed  mint  leaves 

Pour  the  boiling  water  over  the  tea  and 
steep  for  8  minutes.  Strain  the  tea.  Make 
a  syrup  of  the  sugar,  water  and  lemon  juice, 
bring  to  a  boil.  Pour  over  the  mint  leaves 
and  while  still  warm  strain  into  tea.  If 
too  strong  add  warm  water.  Pour  over  ice 
and  serve.  Juice  of  4  oranges  may  be  added 
with  lemon  juice  if  desired.  Serves  30. 


Tom  Collins 

1  fifth  gin 

2  quarts  Tom  Collins  mix 

1  pint  mixed  fresh  citrus  juice 
(12  lemons,  6  limes) 

This  makes  from  1  to  1%  pints. 

Lysbeth  Muncy 

English  Cobbler,  also  a  Richmond  Drink 

Mix  in  a  tall  glass: 

Juice  of  half  a  lemon 
2  teaspoons  of  sugar 

Fill  3/4  full  with  cracked  ice.  Add  2 
ounces  of  sherry  and  a  few  cherries  or 
strawberries  or  other  fruit  in  season. 

Mrs.  Eugenia  Burnett 


Iced  Tea  should  not  cloud  if  placed  in  a 
covered  glass  jar.  If  it  does  become 
cloudy  add  a  spoonful  of  boiling  water. 
Do  not  put  it  into  the  refrigerator. 


Wedding  Punch 

1  quart  brandy 
1%  cups  curacao 

1  quart  lemon  juice 

2  cups  sugar 
1  cup  water 

3  quarts  sauterne 

6  quarts  champagne 

3  quarts  sparkling  water 

Boil  the  sugar  and  water  together  for  5 
minutes.  Cool.  Combine  the  brandy,  curacao, 
lemon  juice,  syrup  and  sauterne  together 
and  let  mellow  in  the  refrigerator  over- 
night. When  ready  to  serve,  pour  over  block 
of  ice  in  punch  bowl,  then  add  champagne 
and  sparkling  water.  Serves  60. 

Edna  Gilchrist 

White  Mountain  Punch 

1  pint  brandy 

4  quarts  sauterne 
4  quarts  soda 

10  lumps  sugar 
Orange  bitters 
Lemon  Peel 

Chill  the  brandy,  sauterne  and  soda.  Drop 
bitters  on  lumps  of  sugar  and  place  in 
bottom  of  punch  bowl.  Place  block  of  ice 
in  punch  bowl.  Pour  over  the  ice  the  brandy, 
sauterne  and  soda.  Add  twisted  lemon  peel. 
Serves  50. 


To  stop  hiccups  eat  slowly  a  teaspoon  of 
granulated  sugar. 


KipipefetzeY»s 


Artichoke  and  Shrimp  Appetizer 

Cold,  cooked  artichokes 
Cooked  shrimp 
Mayonnaise 

Pull  off  the  leaves  of  artichokes.  On 
the  edible  end  put  a  swirl  of  mayonnaise 
and  on  the  mayonnaise  put  one  shrimp. 
Arrange  these  on  a  large  round  platter. 
Colorful  and  delicious. 

Beth  Gawthrop 

Avocado  Appetizer 

3  avocados,  peeled,  halved,  stoned 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

3  Tablespoons  sugar 

3  Tablespoons  vinegar 

3  Tablespoons  catsup 

3  Tablespoons  Worcestershire  sauce 

Sprinkle  of  black  pepper 

Place  butter,  sugar,  vinegar,  catsup, 
Worcestershire,  pepper  in  a  saucepan 
and  heat  until  butter  is  melted.  Stir 
well.  Arrange  avocado  on  lettuce  with 
cut  side  up.  Pour  hot  sauce  into  hole. 
Serve  at  once.  Serve  with  herb  Melba 
toast .  Serves  6 . 

Phyllis  Herndon 


Beer  Cheese 

1  lb.  sharp  cheddar  cheese 

1  lb.  Swiss  cheese 

1  clove  garlic,  smashed 

1  teaspoon  dry  mustard 

1  or  2  teaspoons  Worcestershire 

1  cup  beer 

Grate  cheese,  mix  with  garlic,  mustard 
and  Worcestershire.  Gradually  beat  in 
beer.  Store  in  crock  in  refrigerator. 
Serve  at  room  temperature  on  rye  bread 


Batter  Shrimp 

1  lb .  cooked  and  cleaned  shrimp 

1  cup  flour 

lh    to  2  cups  beer 

To  the  flour,  add  enough  beer  to  make  a 
medium  heavy  batter.   Dip  the  shrimp  in 
the  batter,  drain  slightly  and  fry  in 
deep  fat  until  browned.   Serve  hot  with 
tartar  sauce  or  tomato  cocktail  sauce. 

Dee  Newman 


Decorate  your  hors  d'oeuvre  tray  with 
TOMATO  FLOWERS.  Cut  rather  small  peeled 
tomatoes  into  five  sections,  cutting  only 
3/4  of  the  way  to  the  stem  end.  Spread  out 
the  petals  and  make  a  round  in  the  center 
of  hard  boiled  egg  yolk  put  through  a 
strainer  or  sieve. 


Broccoli  Dip 

2  packages  frozen  broccoli,  chopped 

1  large  onion,  chopped 
4  Tablespoons  butter 

2  rolls  garlic  cheese 

1  3-oz.  can  mushrooms,  chopped 

1  can  mushroom  soup 

Red  pepper  and  salt  to  taste 

Cook  broccoli,  drain  well.   Saute 
onions  and  mushrooms  in  butter.   Place 
in  top  of  double  boiler,  add  garlic 
cheese,  broccoli  and  soup.   Mix  well. 
Add  salt  and  pepper  and  heat  until 
cheese  is  melted 
corn  chips . 


Serve  hot  with 


Frances  Cordell 


Cheese  Ball 

8  oz.  package  cream  cheese 

1  jar  Borden's  pimiento  cheese 

Dash  of  tabasco  sauce 

Dash  of  Worcestershire  sauce 

Dash  of  garlic  salt 

Chopped  pecans 

Beat  the  ingredients  together  until 
smooth.   Place  in  covered  bowl  in  the 
refrigerator  until  f;rm.   Form  into  a 
ball  and  roll  in  chopped  pecans. 


Martha  Anne  Helms 


Cheese  Krispies 

2  sticks  butter,  softened 

2  cups  shredded  sharp  cheese  (^  lb.) 

^  teaspoon  cayenne 

2  cups  flour 

2  cups  Rice  Krispies 

Cream  the  butter  and  cheese  and  flour. 
Stir  in  Rice  Krispies  and  cayenne.  Roll 
in  balls  and  flatten  on  cookie  sheet. 


Bake  at  375°  for  10  minutes 


Store  in 


airtight  container. 

Sesame  Bread  Sticks 

1  package  refrigerated  biscuits 
1  s  tick  but  ter 

1  Tablespoon  toasted  sesame  seeds 

Preheat  oven  to  450°.   Melt  butter.   Roll 
each  biscuit  into  an  8"  stick.   Pour  half 
the  butter  into  a  9"  square  pan.   Place 
dough  sticks  side  by  side  in  pan.   Pour 
remaining  butter  over  top.   Sprinkle 
seeds  on  top.   Bake  10-12  minutes. 

Judy  Lightfoot 

Sardine  Spread  or  Dip 

2  cans  sardines  in  oil 

4  Tablespoons  lemon  juice 
4  Tablespoons  mayonnaise 
2  hard-cooked  eggs,  minced 
2  teaspoons  prepared  mustard 

Combine  all  ingredients  in  blender  and 
blend  till  smooth. 


Phyllis  Cohn 


Cheese  Spread 


1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

H,    cup  chopped  stuffed  olives 
-4  cup  chopped  green  peppers 

2  Tablespoons  chopped  parsley 
4  oz .  blue  cheese,  crumbled 

4  oz.  sweet  butter 

8  oz.  cream  cheese 

Jg  teaspoon  paprika 

1  teaspoon  hot  sauce 

1  Tablespoon  Worcestershire  sauce 

Blend  till  smooth  and  serve  at  room

Cheese  Wafers 

1  lb  .  grated  sharp  cheddar  cheese 
\    lb.  butter  or  margarine 

2  cups  flour 

1  teaspoon  salt 

\    teaspoon  red  pepper 

Cream  butter  or  margarine.  Mix  the  salt  and 
pepper  with  the  flour  and  add  this  to  the 
shortening.  Add  grated  cheese  and  knead  un- 
til well  blended.  Chill  the  dough  and  cookie 
sheets  for  several  hours,  preferably  over- 
night. Run  dough  through  cookie  press,  onto 
the  chilled  cookie  sheet.  Place  pecan  half 
on  each  wafer  and  bake  at  400°  for  10  minutes 
or  vuntil  golden.  (These  may  also  be  made  like 
refrigerator  cookies  and  sliced.) 


Dorothy  Jester 


Dip 

1  3-oz .  package  cream  cheese 

1  Tablespoon  grated  onion 

lh    Tablespoons  fresh  lemon  juice 
Dash  of  nutmeg 

2  egg  yolks,  hard  cooked  and  sieved 

1  jar  caviar,  black  or  red 

Cream  the  cheese  until  smooth.  Add  the 
onion,  lemon  juice  and  nutmeg.  Refrigerate 
24  hours.  Cover  with  caviar  and  egg  yolks. 

Iren  Marik 

Dried  Beef  Log 

5  oz .  chipped  beef,  cut  fine  with 

kitchen  shears 
8  oz.  cream  cheese 

2  Tablespoons  blue  cheese 
1  Tablespoon  grated  onion 

1  Tablespoon  prepared  horseradish 

Parsley 

Thin  rye  bread  of  rye  crackers 

Blend  the  cheeses,  onion  and  horseradish 
well.  Form  into  a  log,  6nx2".  Roll  in 
chopped  parsley.  Chill.  Spread  mixture 
on  very  thin  rye  bread  or  crackers.  Bake 
5  minutes  in  450°  oven. 

Dot  Calkins  Wilder

Ham  and  Egg  Spread 

2/3  cup  ground  ham,  boiled  or  baked 
3  hard  boiled  eggs 

2  teaspoons  minced  onion 

%  teaspoon  dry  mustard  mixed  with 

3  teaspoons  water 
1  teaspoon  catsup 
Mayonnaise,  enough  to  moisten 

Put  ham,  eggs  and  onions  through  meat 
grinder.  Mix  all  other  ingredients  to- 
gether and  add  to  ham.  Moisten  with 
mayonnaise.  Use  on  triscuits  or  melba 
rounds  as  canapes  or  for  sandwich  filling 

Anne  Wheaton

6  slices  thin 
Soft  butter 
Fines  herbes 


sliced  bread 


Toast  bread  slowly  until  brown.  Spread 
with  soft  butter  mixed  with  herbs.  Set 
in  low  oven  for  5  minutes.  Serves  6. 

Phyllis  Herndon 


Fines  herbes  -  a  mixture  of  parsley, 
chives,  tarragon  and  chervil

Liptauer  Cheese 

8  heaping  Tablespoons  creamy  cottage  cheese 

3  oz  .  cream  cheese 

h.    medium  onion,  grated 

1%  teaspoons  capers 

3/4  teaspoon  caraway  seeds 

1  teaspoon  anchovy  paste 

%  teaspoon  dry  mustard 

^  teaspoon  paprika

Marinated  Whole  Mushrooms 

3  6-oz.  cans  whole  mushrooms,  drained 

1  Tablespoon  olive  oil 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

h    teaspoon  thyme 

1  to  2  bay  leaves 

2/3  cup  tarragon  vinegar 

1/3  cup  water 

In  a  large  jar  mix  all  the  ingredients  ex- 
cept the  mushrooms.  Shake  well.  Pour  over 
the  mushrooms,  cover  and  refrigerate  from 
1  to  2  hours.  Remove  the  bay  leaves  before 
serving . 


12 


Marinated  Mushrooms 


lb.  mushrooms  or 

4-oz.  can  of  whole  caps 

large  onion,  sliced 


cup  water 

cup  wine  vinegar  or 
vinegar  to  taste 
h,    teaspoon  salt 
10  peppercorns 
10  whole  allspice 
2  bay  leaves 


Combine  raw  mushrooms,  onion,  salt  and  water 
Simmer  tightly  covered  until  mushrooms  are 
done  -  15-20  minutes.  Add  vinegar,  spices 
and  bay  leaves.  Boil  a  few  minutes.  Cool 
and  transfer  mushrooms  to  a  glass  jar,  seal 
and  refrigerate. 

For  canned  mushrooms,  prepare  the  marinade, 
let  boil  a  few  minutes.  Add  mushrooms  and 
simmer  for  2  minutes.  Leave  mushrooms  in 
marinade  in  the  refrigerator  for  24  hours 
before  serving. 

Aleksandra  Gruzinska 

Shrimp  and  Cheese  Dip 

%    lb.  cooked,  shelled  shrimp 

1  cup  cottage  cheese 

2  teaspoons  grated  onion 
1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 

1  Tablespoon  Worcestershire 
4  Tablespoons  sour  cream 

Chop  the  shrimp  finely.  Add  cheese,  onion, 
lemon  juice,  Worcestershire  and  sour  cream. 
Add  salt  and  pepper  to  taste. 

Audrey  Betts 


13 


Pate  de  Foie  Gras  (Chopped  Livers) 

2  lbs.  chicken  or  baby  beef  livers 
4  hard-boiled  eggs 

3  onions,  medium  size 
Corn  oil 

Place  sufficient  corn  oil  in  frying  pan  to 
cover.   Saute  onions  and  liver  together  till 
done.   Grind  them  with  hard-boiled  eggs. 
Then  mix  together  with  food  chopper  or  fork 
until  eggs  are  well  blended  and  mixture  is 
of  a  semi-paste  consistency. 

Serve  on  crackers  or  use  as  a  main  dish 
with  tomatoes,  pickles,  mustard  and  bread. 

Phyllis  Cohn 


Peanut  Sticks 

10  slices  white  bread,  trimmed  and  cut 

into  4  fingers  each 
1  cup  smooth  peanut  butter 
1  cup  salad  oil 

In  a  250°  oven,  dry  out  the  fingers  of 
bread  and  the  crusts  on  a  cookie  sheet, 
until  crisp  but  not  brown  (25-30  minutes). 
Turn  once.   Roll  out  the  crusts  to  make 
crumbs . 

Mix  the  peanut  butter  and  oil  and  heat  at 
low  temperature  till  smooth.   Dip  the  dried 
fingers  in  the  mixture  and  roll  in  crumbs. 
These  sticks  keep  well  in  a  tightly  closed 
container . 

Mrs.  Fielding  Rogers

h    cup  sherry

Tuna  Pate 

8  oz .  cream  cheese,  softened 

2  Tablespoons  chili  sauce 

2  Tablespoons  snipped  parsley 

1  teaspoon  instant  minced  onion 
h.    teaspoon  hot  pepper  sauce 

2  7-oz.  cans  tuna,  drained 

Blend  all  ingredients  together  and  pack  in 
4-cup  mold.  Chill  at  least  3  hours.  Unmold 
and  serve  with  crackers. 

Dip  for  Vegetables,  Crab  or  Shrimp 

1  cup  mayonnaise 

1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 

1  teaspoon  curry  powder 

Jg  teaspoon  minced  onion 

5g  teaspoon  Worcestershire 

\    teaspoon  red  pepper  sauce 

\    cup  chili  sauce 

Salt  and  pepper  to  taste 

Combine  all  ingredients  and  chill. 

Ginny  Kay  Baldwin  Cox

Water  Chestnuts  and  Bacon 


12  water  chestnuts 

8  slices  bacon 

^  cup  dark  brown  sugar 

%  cup  catsup 

Toothpicks 


Wrap  each  chestnut  half  in  1/3  slice 
bacon.  Secure  with  toothpick.  Brown 
in  oven  until  bacon  is  cooked  and  crisp. 
Pour  off  fat.  Marinate  for  several  hours 
or  overnight  in  sugar  and  catsup.  Before 
serving,  heat  in  350°  oven. 

Blair  Both 

Vegetable  Dip 

1  cup  mayonnaise 

3  teaspoons  soy  sauce 

1  teaspoon  ginger 

1  teaspoon  vinegar 

2  Tablespoons  onion  juice  or  minced  onion 
2  Tablespoons  milk  or  half  and  half 

Combine  ingredients,  stir  until  smooth, 
refrigerate  until  ready  to  serve.  Serve 
with  raw  cauliflower  flowerets,  zucchini 
strips,  carrot  strips,  celery  strips,  etc 

Julie  Jacobsen 


Cucumbers,  peeled  and  cut  into  2"  sticks 
make  good  appetizers  if  sprinkled  with  a 
seasoned  salt  such  as  Krazy  Mixed  up  Salt

Avocado  Soup 

2  large  avocados 

4  cups  chicken  broth 

1  cup  non-dairy  creamer 

1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 

3/4  teaspoon  salt 

h,    teaspoon  Worcestershire  sauce 

Pepper 

Pars  ley 

Combine  avocado  and  2  cups  of  the  broth 
in  a  blender  until  smooth.   Combine  with 
remaining  ingredients  in  saucepan,  beat 
with  wire  whisk  to  blend.   Bring  to  a 
boil  stirring  constantly.   Garnish  with 
slices  of  avocado  and  parsley.   Serves  6 

Elizabeth  Carr 


Cold  Buttermilk  Soup 

lh    pounds  shrimp,  cooked  and  minced 

%  medium  cucumber,  finely  diced 

1  Tablespoon  fresh  dill 

1  Tablespoon  prepared  mustard 

1  teaspoon  salt 

1  teaspoon  sugar 

1  quart  buttermilk 

Mix  together  shrimp,  cucumber  and  seasoning 
Stir  in  buttermilk  and  chill  thoroughly. 
Serves  6. 

Patty  Lynas  Ford

Beef  Soup 

Soup  bones,  shin  type,  enough  to  yield 
2  lbs .  of  meat 

4  cups  water 
^  cup  barley 
1  cup  carrots 
1  large  onion 

1  cup  celery,  with  leaves* 

^  teaspoon  thyme 

^  teaspoon  marjoram 

1  bay  leaf 

5  peppercorns 

1  Tablespoon  salt 
1  Tablespoon  sugar 
1  can  tomatoes 
1  can  tomato  juice 

Cut  meat  off  bones  and  brown  in  fat.  Add 
4  cups  water  and  cook  meat  and  bones  in 
pressure  cooker  for  15  minutes.  Add  other 
ingredients  except  tomato  juice.  Cook 
another  10  minutes  in  pressure  cooker.  Add 

1  can  tomato  juice  and  serve  hot. 

Fannie  Peirce 
Blender  Vichyssoise 

2  cans  frozen  or  canned  potato  soup 
2  cups  milk 

Chives 

Freshly  ground  black  pepper 

Combine  soup  and  milk  and  bring  to  a  boil, 
but  do  not  let  them  boil.  Cool.  Put  in 
blender  and  blend  till  smooth.  Chill  4-5 
hours.  Serve  with  chopped  chives  and  fresh 
pepper.

Cream  of  Chicken  and  Cucumber  Soup 

1  can  cream  of  mushroom  soup 
1  can  cream  of  chicken  soup 
1  can  water 

1  cup  peeled,  diced  cucumber 

2  Tablespoons  butter 

2*  Tablespoons  grated  onion 
\    to  Sg  teaspoon  curry  powder 
H    cup  top  milk  or  light  cream 
Salt,  pepper,  paprika 

Melt  butter,  add  curry,  onion  and  cucumber. 
Simmer,  covered,  about  5  minutes,  or  until 
cucumber  is  tender.   Add  soups,  water,  milk 
and  heat.   Do  not  boil.   Serve  hot  or  cold. 

Helen  McMahon 

Shrimp  Chowder 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

3  onions,  chopped  or  sliced 

5  medium  potatoes 

1^  cups  water 

2  lbs.  shrimp,  cooked,  cleaned 

Pepper  to  taste 

1  package  frozen  peas,  cooked 

1  can  corn 

1  quart  milk 

h    lb.  Velveeta  cheese 

1  teaspoon  salt 

Saute  onions  in  butter  in  large  kettle. 
Peel  and  dice  potatoes.   Add  potatoes, 
seasonings  and  water  to  kettle.   Cook 
about  10  minutes,  until  potatoes  are  done. 
Add  shrimp,  drain  peas  and  corn  and  add. 
Melt  cheese  in  milk  and  add.   Serve  hot. 
Can  be  frozen  and  reheated.   Serves  6.

Sour  Cream

Corn  Chowder 

8  oz.  salt  pork,  diced 
2  onions,  chopped 
%    cup  chopped  celery  tops 
H   bay  leaf,  crumbled 

2  Tablespoons  flour 
4  cups  water 

3  cups  diced  potatoes 

1  can  cream-style  corn 

2  cups  evaporated  milk 
Salt  and  pepper 
Chopped  parsley 
Paprika 

In  large  kettle,  cook  salt  pork  until 
browned  and  crisp.   Remove  pork,  pour 
off  all  but  3  Tablespoons  fat.   Add  onions, 
celery  and  bay  leaf.   Cook  5  minutes.   Blend 
in  flour.   Add  water  and  potatoes.   Bring  to 
a  boil  and  simmer,  covered,  15  minutes.   Add 
corn  and  milk.   Heat  well.   Season.   Add  pork 
and  serve  with  parsley  and  paprika.   Makes 
about  2  quarts.

Cheese  Fondue 


cup  milk 

cup  soft  bread  crumbs 

teaspoon  salt 

cup  grated  cheese 

Tablespoon  butter 

eggs ,  separated 


Into  the  top  of  a  double  boiler  put  the 
milk,  bread  crumbs,  salt,  cheese,  butter 
and  egg  yolks.  Blend  well.  Beat  the  egg 
whites  till  stiff.  Fold  into  the  cheese 
mixture  and  pour  into  a  buttered  baking 
dish.  Bake  20  minutes  in  350°  oven. 
Serves  6 . 

Mrs.  J.  R.  Bulgin 


Use  a  metal  fondue  pot  if  cooking  beef 
fondue  with  hot  oil.   The  high  tempera- 
ture of  the  oil  may  break  pottery  or 
ceramic  pots.   A  teaspoon  of  salt  added 
to  the  oil  will  reduce  the  spatter. 


The  color  of  an  egg  has  nothing  to  do  with 
its  quality.   Fresh  eggs  are  rough  and 
chalky.   Old  eggs  are  smooth  and  shiny. 


To  keep  cheese  from  getting  mildewed, 
butter  the  open  sides.

Eggs  a  la  Bour guignonne 

2  cups  light  red  wine 

2  shallots 

1  bay  leaf 

1  sprig  parsley 

h,    teaspoon  thyme 

6  slices  bread  rubbed  with  split  clove 

of  garlic 
6  eggs 

1  Tablespoon  flour 

2  Tablespoons  butter 

Boil  the  wine  in  frying  pan  for  5  minutes 
with  herbs  and  seasonings.  While  wine  is 
cooking,  saute*  bread  in  a  little  butter, 
browning  both  sides.  Place  on  a  hot  plat- 
ter and  keep  warm.  Poach  eggs  in  seasoned 
wine  and  transfer  to  bread.  Cook  liquor 
until  reduced  to  1/3  of  its  original 
quantity.  Cream  1  Tablespoon  butter  with 
flour  and  add  to  liquor  and  cook,  stirring 
until  thickened.  Add  1  more  Tablespoon  but 
ter  and  correct  seasonings.  Strain  over 
eggs  .

Pizza 


1  package  granulated  yeast 

1  cup  warm  water 
4  cups  flour 

3/4  teaspoon  salt 

2  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

1  small  can  tomato  paste 
lb.  mozarella  cheese 
chopped  green  pepper 
can  Italian  tomatoes, 
lb  .  ground  meat 
lb.  mushrooms,  sauted 
Tablespoons  butter 


drained 


in 


Mix  the  yeast  in  the  water.  Add  to  the  flour 
and  salt.  Knead  for  15  minutes.  Add  olive 
oil  and  knead  till  smooth.  Cover  and  put  in 
warm  place  till  double  in  bulk.  Roll  or 
stretch  to  fit  2  pizza  pans.  Grease  pans 
with  olive  oil.  Cover  dough  with  tomato 
paste,  cheese  (grated),  green  pepper, 
tomatoes,  ground  meat,  and  mushrooms. 
Sprinkle  with  salt  and  pepper  and  bake 
at  400-450°  till  crust  is  light  brown. 
Serves  8 . 

Emily  Whaley 


To  divide  an  egg,  beat  it,  then  measure  it 
in  a  measuring  cup. 


Cook  eggs,  cheese  and  cheese  dishes  slowly. 
High  cooking  temperatures  make  them  rubbery

Quiche 


9"  unbaked  pie  shell 

10  slices  bacon,  crisp,  crumbled 

1  cup  cubed  cheese 

lb.  mushrooms,  chopped 
Tablespoon  chopped  onions 
Tablespoon  bacon  drippings 
large  eggs,  beaten  slightly 
cups  whipping  cream 
teaspoon  pepper 

3/4  teaspoon  salt 

Pinch  sugar 

Dash  cayenne 


Bake  pie  shell  for  5  minutes  at  325°. 
Saute  mushrooms  and  onion  in  bacon  drip- 
pings. Cover  pastry  with  cheese,  onions 
and  bacon.  Combine  remaining  ingredients 
and  pour  over  the  top.  Bake  at  450°  for 
10  minutes,  then  reduce  the  heat  to  325° 
and  bake  until  inserted  knife  comes  out 
clean,  25-30  minutes.  Serves  6.

Olive  Quiche 

1  cup  chopped  ripe  olives 

4  slices  bacon 

\    cup  chopped  onion 

1^  cups  milk 

1  teaspoon  salt 

Sg  teaspoon  dry  mustard 
3  eggs 

2  cups  grated  sharp  cheese 
9"  pie  shell,  unbaked 

Cut  bacon  in  small  bits  and  fry  till  crisp. 
Remove  from  pan.  Pour  off  all  except  1  Table 
spoon  fat  and  cook  onion  slowly  in  bacon  fat 
till  transparent.  Add  milk,  salt,  mustard 
and  heat  till  scalded.  Beat  eggs  lightly, 
add  cheese  slowly,  add  hot  milk.  Blend  in 
olives  and  bacon.  Pour  into  pastry  shell. 
Bake  at  375°  for  25  minutes  until  set  in 
center.  Cool  5  or  10  minutes  before  serving. 
Serves  6 . 

Onion  Quiche 


9"  unbaked  pie  shell 

1  medium  onion,  chopped 

8  strips  bacon,  fried  crisp 

%    cup  Swiss  cheese,  diced 

h,    cup  ham,  cubed 

1^  cups  light  cream 

h    teaspoon  salt 

h    teaspoon  nutmeg 

4  e  ggs 

1  Tablespoon  butter 

Saute  the  onion  in  butter  till  transparent. 
Spread  crumbled  bacon  on  pie  shell,  sprinkle 
cheese  and  ham  over  bacon.  Place  cream,  eggs 
and  spices  in  blender.  Mix  thoroughly.  Pour 
over  bacon,  ham  and  cheese  in  pie  shell. 
Bake  at  350°  for  30  minutes  or  until  set  and 
golden  brown.  Serves  6.

Salmon  Quiche 


2

9" 


Tablespoons  butter 
Tablespoons  chopped  onion 
lb.  can  red  salmon 
Tablespoons  fresh  dill 
teaspoon  black  pepper 
cup  salmon  liquid 
cup  heavy  cream 
eggs 
unbaked  pie  shell 


Preheat  oven  to  375°.  Bake  pie  shell  for 
10  minutes.  Melt  butter  and  saute  onions 
till  tender.  Mash  salmon,  dill,  pepper, 
liquid  and  onion  till  well-mixed.  Pour 
scalded  cream  over  eggs  while  beating. 
Gradually  beat  egg  mixture  into  salmon 
mixture.  Pour  into  pie  shell.  Bake  30 


minutes 


at  375°  until  set.  Serves  6 


To  clarify  butter  or  margarine  melt  it  in 
a  small  pan  over  hot  water  or  in  a  double 
boiler  until  milk  solids  settle  to  the  bot- 
tom of  pan.  Skim  off  any  foam.  Strain  the 
rest  through  a  fine  sieve  or  several  layers 
of  cheese  cloth  into  container  with  tightly 
fitting  lid.  The  sediment  may  be  mixed  with 
foam  and  used  for  vegetables. 

To  clarify  bacon  fat  for  cooking,  pour 
slightly  cooled  fat  into  a  can  with  cold 
water.  Burnt  part  will  drop  to  the  bottom 
and  bacon  fat  can  be  removed  and  stored  in 
the  refrigerator.

Spinach  and  Onion  Pie 

9"  unbaked  pie  shell 
1  egg  white 

1  cup  sliced  onions 

2  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

2  packages  chopped  spinach 

4  eggs 

\\    cups  light  cream 

h    cup  grated  Parmesan  cheese 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

1  teaspoon  salt 

1  teaspoon  dry  mustard 

%    teaspoon  nutmeg 

Dash  cayenne  pepper 

Thaw  spinach  and  drain  it.  Prick  the  pie 
shell  with  a  fork  over  base  and  side. 
Brush  all  over  with  egg  white.  Leave  at 
room  temperature  to  dry,  10  minutes. 
Saute  onion  in  olive  oil  for  4  or  5 
minutes  until  just  tender.  Combine 
spinach  with  onion.  In  separate  bowl, 
gently  beat  together  the  eggs,  milk. 
Stir  in  onions,  spinach,  cheese,  garlic, 
salt,  mustard  and  cayenne.  Pour  into  pie 
shell.  Bake  at  375°  about  30  to  35  minutes 
or  until  inserted  knife  comes  out  clean. 
Let  set  5  minutes  before  serving.  Serves  6

Supper  Pudding 

4  slices  white  bread,  buttered 

1  cup  grated  cheese 

2  Tablespoons  crumbled  bacon 

1  teaspoon  seasoned  salt 
4  eggs 

2  cups  milk  or  cream 

Separate  eggs;  beat  yolks  with  milk.  Cut 
bread  in  1"  squares.  Combine  bread,  cheese, 
bacon,  salt.  Add  to  milk  mixture.  Beat  egg 
whites  until  stiff  and  fold  into  bread  mix- 
ture. Pour  into  well-greased  2-quart  cas- 
serole, bake  at  325°  for  45  minutes,  or 
until  firm  and  golden  brown.

Us 


cups  Swiss  cheese,  shredded 


1  can  cream  chicken  soup 
3/4  cup  light  cream 
^  teaspoon  mustard

Asparagus  Casserole 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
2  Tablespoons  flour 

1  cup  milk 
Salt  and  Pepper 

2  Tablespoons  cheddar  cheese 
%    cup  almonds 

2  cans  of  asparagus  spears 
\    cup  buttered  crumbs 

Melt  the  butter,  add  the  flour,  cook  till 
well  blended.   Add  the  milk  slowly  and  cook 
till  thick,  stirring  constantly.   Add  salt 
and  pepper  to  taste.   Add  the  cheese  and 
stir  over  low  heat  till  melted.   Remove 
from  heat  and  add  nuts.   Arrange  the 
asparagus  in  a  shallow  baking  dish.   Pour 
the  sauce  over  the  asparagus.   Top  with 
crumbs  and  brown  in  375°  oven.   Serves  6.

Artichoke-Mushroom  Casserole 

2  cans  artichoke  hearts 

6  oz .  can  broiled  sliced  mushrooms,  drained 

1  envelope  chicken  gravy  mix 

Dash  crushed  thyme 

Dash  crushed  marjoram 

4  oz.  Swiss  cheese,  diced  (1  cup) 

1  Tablespoon  dry  white  wine 

1  cup  buttered  soft  bread  crumbs 

Drain  and  halve  artichokes  and  add  to  mush- 
rooms.  Place  in  1-quart  shallow  casserole. 
In  small  saucepan,  prepare  the  chicken  gravy 
mix  according  to  directions.   Remove  from 
heat.   Add  thyme,  marjoram  and  cheese.   Stir 
just  till  cheese  melts.   Add  wine  and  pour 
over  vegetables.   Top  with  a  wreath  of 
buttered  crumbs.   Bake,  uncovered,  at  350 
for  30  minutes.   Serves  6.

1  can  cream  mushroom  soup 

%  cup  shredded  cheese 

h    cup  mayonnaise 

1  beaten  egg 

H,    cup  milk 

h,    cup  fine  dry  bread  crumbs 

1  Tablespoon  butter,  melted 

Cook  broccoli  according  to  package  direc- 
tions, omitting  salt.   Drain  thoroughly. 
Place  in  a  shallow  baking  dish.   Stir  to- 
gether the  soup  and  cheese.   Gradually  add 
milk,  mayonnaise,  and  beaten  egg  to  the 
soup  mix,  stirring  till  well  blended.   Poi 
over  broccoli  in  baking  dish.   Combine  br 
crumbs  and  melted  butter.   Sprinkle  the 
crumbs  evenly  over  the  casserole.   Bake 
at  350°  for  45  minutes,  till  crumbs  arr 
lightly  browned.   Serves  6.

Bee  f  Casse  role 

2  lb  s .  beef  cubes 

10%  oz  .  can  french  onion  soup 

Burgundy  wine,  optional 

10%  oz .  can  mushroom  soup 

8  oz.  package  noodles,  cooked

Mix  the  beef,  onion  soup  and  mushroom  soup 
together  in  a  casserole  and  bake  at  350°

fare,  add  Burgundy  to  flavor.   Add  mushrooms 
the  last  10  minutes.   If  fresh  mushrooms  are

can  be  made  ahead  and  frozen.   Serves  4-6.

Cheese  Puff

%  teaspoon  salt 

%  teaspoon  dry  mustard

boiler.   Add  the  milk,  cool.   Add  the 
beaten  egg  yolks,  bread  and  seasoning. 
Fpld  in  the  beaten  egg  whites  and  pour 
into  a  well  greased  1%  quart  casserole.

325°  for  45  minutes  or  until  firm. 
Serves  6 .

Cauliflower  Hungarian 

1  large  head  cauliflower 

2  cups  sour  cream 
2  eggs 

2  Tablespoons  flour 
Pinch  salt 

Buttered  bread  crumbs 
Parmesan  cheese 

Break  up  cauliflower  into  flowerlets  and 
soak  in  salted  cold  water.   Cool  the 
cauliflower  in  plenty  of  salted  water  un- 
til soft  but  not  mushy.   Meanwhile  beat 
egg  yolks  and  combine  with  sour  cream, 
salt,  flour  and  beaten  egg  whites.   Put 
cauliflower  in  buttered  baking  dish  and 
pour  over  it  the  cream  mixture.   Top  with 
buttered  bread  crumbs  and  parmesan  cheese 
Bake  at  225°  for  15  or  20  minutes  until 
b  rowned .

Celery  Bake 


1  large  bunch  celery  cut  in 
1  medium  onion,  chopped 

1  green  pepper,  chopped 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
lh    cups  celery  broth 

3  oz,  package  cream  cheese 
3  oz .  package  blue  cheese 
3/4  cup  heavy  cream 

3  Tablespoons  dry  sherry 
Salt  and  pepper 


pieces 


Cook  celery  in  water  till  barely  tender. 
Drain,  reserve  the  broth.   In  a  large 
skillet,  cook  the  onion  and  green  pepper 
in  butter  till  soft.   Blend  in  celery  broth, 
cream  cheese,  blue  cheese,  cream,  sherry, 
salt  and  pepper.   Place  the  celery  in  a 
shallow  baking  dish  and  pour  the  sauce  over 
it.   Bake  15  minutes  at  400°  or  until  thick 
and  bubbly.   Serves  6.

Creamy  Celery  Bake 

4  cups  thinly  sliced  celery 
4  Tablespoons  butter 
3  Tablespoons  flour 
1  teaspoon  salt 

1  cup  milk 

Sg  cup  chopped  mushrooms 

2  Tablespoons  chopped  green  pepper 
2  Tablespoons  chopped  pimiento 

1  cup  shredded  sharp  cheese 

1  cup  soft  bread  crumbs 

2  Tablespoons  butter,  melted 

In  a  skillet,  cook  celery  in  the  4  Tablespoons 
butter  till  tender,  about  5  minutes.  Push 
celery  to  one  side;  stir  in  flour  and  salt. 
Add  milk.  Cook  and  stir  till  mixture  is 
thick  and  bubbly.  Stir  in  mushrooms,  green 
pepper  and  pimiento.  Add  cheese  and  stir 
till  melted.  Pour  into  a  shallow  baking 
dish.  Combine  crumbs  and  butter  and  sprinkle 
over  casserole.  Bake  at  350°  for  20  minutes. 
Serves  8. 

Hominy  Bake 

1  cup  boiling  water 

1  teaspoon  salt 
3/4  cup  hominy 

2  cups  milk 
h    cup  butter 

2  Tablespoons  sugar 
1  egg,  lightly  beaten 

To  the  boiling  water  in  a  saucepan,  add 
slowly  the  salt  and  hominy.  Cook  until  it 
thickens.  Add  milk.  When  liquid  is  absorbed 
remove  from  heat.  Add  butter  and  sugar. 
When  fairly  cool,  add  the  beaten  egg.  Pour 
into  a  greased  casserole  and  bake  1  hour  at 
350°.  Serves  6. 


Mandy  Cronin

Celery  Oriental 

4  cups  sliced  celery 

h    cup  pimiento,  chopped 

5  oz.  can  water  chestnuts,  sliced 
2  Tablespoons  butter,  melted 

%    cup  bread  crumbs 

h    cup  almonds,  thinly  sliced 

10^  oz .  can  cream  of  chicken  soup 


Cook  celery  in  small  amount  salted  boiling 
water  till  barely  tender.   Drain  celery 
and  place  in  1%  quart  casserole.   Add 
pimiento,  water  chestnuts  and  soup.   Stir 
carefully  until  well  blended.   Add  the 
bread  crumbs  to  the  melted  butter  and 
almonds.   Toss.   Sprinkle  crumbs  and  nuts 
over  top  of  casserole.   Bake  at  350   until 
brown,  about  35  minutes.   Serves  6. 


Cheese-Rice 

1  cup  cold  cooked  rice 
3  eggs,  separated 

h    pound  grated  cheese 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
%    cup  milk 

Pinch  of  salt 

Beat  the  egg  whites  until  stiff.   Add  the 
yol.ks  to  the  rice.   Blend  in  the  milk, 
butter  and  cheese.   Stir  well.   Gently 
fold  in  the  beaten  egg  whites,  adding  a 
little  salt  to  taste  and  pour  into  a 
greased  casserole.   Bake  at  300°  for 
45  minutes  or  until  souffle  is  brown 


on  top .   Serves  6 .

h    cup  red  wine

Chicken-Rice  Casserole 

6  chicken  breasts 

1  cup  rice 

1  cup  onion,  chopped 

1  cup  celery,  chopped 

kj  can  cream  of  mushroom  soup 

1  cup  cooked  ham  in  strips 

1  cup  chicken  stock 

Salt,  Pepper,  and  Butter 

1  cup  sherry 

Salad  oil 

Saute  the  rice  in  a  small  amount  of  oil. 
Saute  the  celery  and  onion  and  add  to  the 
rice.   Cook  over  medium  heat  for  10  minutes 
Add  soup  and  ham.   Put  rice  mixture  in  a 
casserole.   Add  stock  and  sherry.   Put  raw 
chicken  breasts  on  top.   Salt,  pepper  and 
butter  the  chicken.   Cover  with  foil. 
Bake  at  350°  for  30  minutes.   Remove 
foil  and  bake  30  minutes  more.   Serves  6. 

Lucy  Lombardi

Vinegar  and  water 

Poultry  seasoning,  or  Thyme 

Celery  salt  or  onion  salt 

Salt 

Pepper 

1  can  mushroom  soup

moistened  in  vinegar  and  water.   Season 
with  salt,  pepper,  poultry  seasoning  or 
thyme,  celery  salt  or  onion  salt.   Place 
in  casserole.   Pour  mushroom  soup  over 
the  chicken  and  cook  at  350°  for  2  hours. 
Serves  4.

Chinese  Shrimp  Casserole 

3/4  lb.  shrimp,  cooked 
^  cup  chopped  celery 

1  cup  chopped  onion 
H    cup  water 

4  oz.  can  sliced  mushrooms 

2  Tablespoons  butter 

3/4  cup  chopped  green  pepper 
6  oz.  can  cashew  nuts,  chopped 

4  oz.  can  pimiento,  chopped 

5  oz.  can  water  chestnuts,  sliced 
3h    Tablespoons  butter 

3^  Tablespoons  flour 
2h    cups  milk 
Salt  and  pepper 

6  oz.  can  Chinese  noodles

pan  until  soft.   Drain.   Fry  mushrooms  lightly 
in  butter,  stir  in  celery-onion  mixture,  green 
pepper,  nuts,  pimiento,  chestnuts,  shrimp. 
Make  cream  sauce  with  butter,  flour,  milk 
and  salt  and  pepper.   Combine  sauce  and  shrimp

of  water.

Moussaka 

2  lbs.  ground  beef  (chuck)  or  lamb 

2-3  large  cloves  of  garlic,  coarsely  chopped 

3  large  potatoes,  thinly  sliced 
3  large  onions,  thinly  sliced 

1  large  eggplant,  sliced 
1^  pints  plain  yoghurt 

2  eggs 

%  cup  milk 

h    cup  freshly  grated  Parmesan  or 

Romano  cheese 
%  teaspoon  baking  powder  (all  purpose) 


teaspoon  ground  mace 


h 

Salt 

Black  pepper,  coarsely  ground  or  cracked 

Olive  oil 

In  a  large  skillet  quickly  brown  the  ground 
meat  in  some  olive  oil  with  the  garlic,  salt 
and  pepper  to  taste.  Set  aside.  In  a  bowl 
beat  together  the  yoghurt,  milk,  eggs,  cheese, 
baking  powder,  mace  and  some  salt  and  pepper. 
Oil  a  large  heavy  casserole,  such  as  a  Dutch 
oven,  with  olive  oil  and  begin  building  the 
Moussaka  by  laying  in  first  a  layer  of  sliced 
potatoes,  lightly  salted,  then  a  layer  of 
sliced  onions,  a  layer  of  ground  meat  (h    the 
amount),  a  layer  of  sliced  eggplant,  a  generou 
layer  of  the  yoghurt  mixture.  Repeat  these 
layers  until  the  ingredients  are  used  or  the 
pot  is  full.  Use  all  the  meat,  eggplant  and 
yoghurt  which  should  top  off  the  stack.  Cover 
the  pot  and  bake  for  about  an  hour  at  350  , 
then  uncover  and  let  the  top  brown  for  15 
or  20  minutes.  Serve  hot  and  with  a  not  too 
fancy  red  wine.  Serves  6-8. 

Calvin  Kentfield

Swiss  Turkey-Ham  Bake 

%  cup  chopped  onions 

2  Tablespoons  butter 

3  Tablespoons  flour 
%  teaspoon  salt 

H,    teaspoon  pepper 

1  cup  evaporated  milk 

2  Tablespoons  sherry 

2  cups  cooked  turkey 

1  cup  cubed  ham 

3  oz .  can  sliced  mushrooms 

5  oz .  can  water  chestnuts,  sliced 

2  oz .  Swiss  cheese,  shredded 
1%  cups  soft  bread  crumbs 

3  Tablespoons  butter,  melted 

Cook  onion  in  butter  till  tender,  add  the 
flour,  salt,  and  pepper.  Stir  and  cook  till 
well  blended.  Add  the  milk  and  sherry.  Cook 
and  stir  till  bubbly.  Add  the  turkey,  ham, 
mushrooms  and  chestnuts.  Pour  into  a  lh 
quart  casserole.  Top  with  shredded  cheese. 
Mix  the  bread  crumbs  with  melted  butter  and 
sprinkle  over  casserole.  Bake  at  400   for 
25  minutes.  Serves  6. 

Ham-Noodle  Casserole 


3  cups  cooked  ham,  cubed 

8  oz.  package  noodles 

h    cup  grated  onion 

2  cups  sour  cream 

3/4  cup  buttered  bread  crumbs 


Grease  2-quart  casserole  lightly.  Layer  the 
noodles  which  have  been  cooked  according  to 
the  package  instructions,  ham  and  sour  cream 
mixed  with  the  onion  (3  layers).  Top  with 
buttered  crumbs  and  heat  thoroughly  at  350° 
for  20-30  minutes.  Serves  6.

Pork  Chop  Casserole 

4  thick  double  pork  chops 

4  thick  slices  onion 

4  thick  slices  tomato 

4  rings  pepper 

\    clove  garlic 

Jg  cup  raw  rice 

2  bouillon  cubes 

2H    cups  water 

Salt,  pepper,  parsley 

Trim  excess  fat  from  chops  and  brown  quickly. 
Transfer  enough  rendered  fat  to  deep  casserole 
to  prevent  sticking,  discard  balance.  Arrange 
chops  in  one  layer,  cover  each  chop  with  slice 
of  onion,  then  tomato,  then  pepper.  Dribble 
raw  rice  in  hollows.  Add  bouillon  cubes  to 
water.  Dissolve.  Add  salt  and  pepper,  garlic 
and  parsley  and  pour  over  chops.  Cook  at  350 
for  lh    hours.  Serve  with  tart  tossed  salad. 
Se  rves  4 . 

Estelle  Beecher 


Turkey  and  Broccoli 

1  large  bunch  broccoli  or  2  packages  of  frozen 

6-8  large  slices  of  turkey 

h    cup  melted  butter 

1  10^  oz .  can  condensed  cream  of  chicken  soup 

1  cup  sour  cream 

1  7-oz.  jar  whole  drained  pimientos 

3/4  cup  grated  Swiss  cheese 

Cook  broccoli  and  arrange  it  in  a  shallow 
casserole  ( 8"xl2"x2 " ) .  Place  turkey  on  top 
and  pour  melted  butter  over  it.  Next  blend 
undiluted  soup  and  sour  cream  and  pour  them 
over  the  turkey  and  broccoli.  Place  pimientos 
on  top  and  sprinkle  with  cheese.  Bake  at  400° 
for  25  minutes.  Serves  3. 


Laura  Buckham

Pilaf 

1  cup  rice 

2%    cups  shrimp  stock 

1  medium  sized  onion,  grated 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

Salt  and  white  pepper  to  taste 

Lightly  brown  the  onion  in  butter.  Add  water, 
salt,  pepper  and  bring  to  a  boil.  Add  washed, 
drained  rice.  When  this  comes  to  a  boil,  stir 
well,  cover  pan,  lower  heat  and  simmer  for 
about  half  hour  until  all  liquid  is  gone. 
Stir  lightly  with  a  large  fork  to  separate 
grains  of  rice.  Cover  saucepan  with  a  double 
piece  of  paper  toweling  and  put  lid  over 
that  until  ready  to  serve.  Keep  in  a  warm 
place.  Serve  with  shrimp.  Serves  6. 

Penny  Lagakos

1  cup  water 

2  cups  milk 

2  Tablespoons  cornstarch 
2  Tablespoons  grated  onion 
^  stick  butter 
1  teaspoon  sugar 

Cook  squash  in  boiling  water  till  tender. 
Add  other  ingredients.  The  mixture  will  be 
quite  thin.  Butter  a  casserole  and  pour  in 
the  mixture.  Bake  at  350°  for  30  minutes. 
It  should  rise  like  a  souffle.  Serves  6.

Potatoes  Whipped  with  Cheese 

6  cups  cooked,  whipped  potatoes 

h    lb.  butter 

6  oz .  cream  cheese 

1  green  pepper,  chopped 

1  bunch  scallions,  sliced 

1  small  can  pimiento,  chopped 
h    cup  grated  cheese 

%    cup  Parmesan  cheese 
h    teaspoon  saffron 

To  the  potatoes,  add  butter,  cream  cheese, 
green  pepper,  scallions,  pimiento,  grated 
cheese,  Parmesan  cheese  and  saffron,  beat- 
ing constantly.  The  mixture  should  be  fairly 
moist.  If  not,  add  a  bit  of  cream  and  more 
butter.  Pile  into  casserole  and  bake  un- 
covered at  350°  for  30  minutes.  Serves  10-12. 

Squash  Casserole 

2  cups  summer  squash,  white 
2  cups  zucchini,  green 

2  cups  crooked  neck  squash,  yellow 

^  cup  chopped  onion 

Butter 

Salt 

Pepper 

h    cup  shredded  cheddar  cheese 

In  a  buttered  2  quart  casserole,  layer  first 
the  white  squash,  half  the  onion,  salt,  pepper 
and  butter,  then  the  green  squash,  the  rest  of 
the  onion,  salt,  pepper  and  butter,  then  the 
yellow  squash.  Top  with  the  cheese.  Bake, 
covered,  at  350°  for  30-40  minutes,  then 
uncover  and  bake  for  10  more  minutes  to 
brown  cheese.  Serves  6-8.

Squash  Casserole  de  luxe 

3  lbs.  yellow  squash 

1  medium  onion,  chopped 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
Salt  and  pepper  to  taste 
1  cup  sour  cream 

1  small  package  slivered  almonds 
1  cup  buttered  bread  crumbs 

Cook  squash  and  mash  with  potato  masher. 
Saute  onion  in  butter.  Add  onion  to  squash. 
Warm  the  sour  cream  and  add  to  squash.  Brown 
onions  in  300°  oven  and  add  to  squash.  Add 
salt  and  pepper.  Thoroughly  mix  ingredients 
and  place  in  casserole.  Sprinkle  bread 
crumbs  on  top.  Heat  thoroughly  in  300° 
oven  before  serving.  Serves  6-8.

Rolled  Shoulder  Steak 

1  beef  shoulder,  h"    thick,  cut  in  6  slices 

2  cups  dry  bread  crumbs 

1  egg,  slightly  beaten 

2  Tablespoons  shortening,  melted 

1  teaspoon  onion  juice 
h    teaspoon  salt 

Dash  of  poultry  seasoning 
Dash  of  paprika 

2  Tablespoons  water 
1  cup  beef  stock 

Pound  each  slice  of  steak  with  a  cleaver  or 
heavy  bottle.  Stir  egg  into  crumbs,  add 
other  ingredients  except  shortening.  Spread 
layer  of  stuffing  on  a  piece  of  meat,  roll 
up,  tie  securely  and  do  the  same  with  the 
other  slices  of  meat.  Brown  each  roll  in 
shortening  in  heavy  skillet.  Add  1  cup  of 
stock  and  simmer  on  top  of  stove  for  1  hour 
Serves  6. 

Naomi  Ossar

Easy  Steak  and  Mushrooms 

1^-2  lbs.  round  steak 
3-oz.  can  button  mushrooms 
1  can  cream  of  mushroom  soup 
1  Tablespoon  butter  ■ 
1  Tablespoon  flour 
Freshly  ground  pepper 

Brown  the  drained  mushrooms  in  butter.   Set 
aside.   Brown  the  steak  in  butter.   Pour 
soup,  mixed  with  flour,  over  the  steak. 
Add  mushrooms  and  pepper.   Cover  and  simmer 
over  low  heat  until  fork  tender  (1-2  hours). 
Serves  4. 

Judy  Campbell  Lightfoot 

Filet  mignon,  Charleville 

^  lb.  mushrooms,  sliced 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

1  Tablespoon  each  Brandy,  madeira,  sherry 

1  Tablespoon  flour 

h,    cup  sweet  butter 

1  Tablespoon  Dijon  mustard 

Salt 

4  1"  slices  filet  mignon 

Saute  mushrooms  for  5  minutes  in  butter.   Add 
brandy  and  wines,  ignite,  let  flames  die  down 
Sprinkle  flour  over  mushrooms,  stir  in  sweet 
butter  till  melted.   Add  mustard.   Continue 
stirring  until  sauce  thickens.   Keep  warm 
over  low  heat.   Heat  iron  skillet  very  hot 
and  sprinkle  with  salt.   Pan  broil  filet 
slices,  4  minutes  on  first  side,  3  on  second 
(medium  rare).   Serve  filets  on  hot  plates 
and  spoon  sauce  over  them.   Serves  4. 

Kathy  Barnes

Sweet-Sour  Beef 

^  cup  flour  1 

1  teaspoon  salt 

Dash  pepper  | 

2  lbs.  cubed  beef  stew  meat  • 
%  cup  cooking  oil 

1  cup  water  i 

Jg  cup  catsup  ' 

\    cup  brown  sugar 

\    cup  vinegar  i 

1  Tablespoon  Worcestershire  " 

1  teaspoon  salt 

1  large  onion,  chopped  t 

3  carrots,  cut  in  3/4"  pieces                    ' 

Combine  flour,  1  teaspoon  salt  and  pepper.      [ 
Coat  meat  with  flour  mixture.  In  large  skillet," 
brown  meat  on  all  sides  in  hot  oil.  Combine 
water,  catsup,  brown  sugar,  vinegar,  Worcester-] 
shire  and  1  teaspoon  salt.  Stir  into  browned 
meat.  Add  onion.  Cover  and  cook  over  low  heat 
for  45  minutes,  stirring  once  or  twice.  Add

til meat  and  carrots  are  tender.  Serve  over 
noodles.  Serves  4.

aside.   Brown  the  steak  in  butter.   Pour 
soup,  mixed  with  flour,  over  the  steak. 
Add  mushrooms  and  pepper.   Cover  and  simmer 
over  low  heat  until  fork  tender  (1-2  hours) . 
Serves  4 . 

Judy  Campbell  Lightfoot 

Filet  mignon,  Charleville 

^  lb.  mushrooms,  sliced 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

1  Tablespoon  each  Brandy,  madeira,  sherry 

1  Tablespoon  flour 

h    cup  sweet  butter 

1  Tablespoon  Dijon  mustard 

Salt 

4  1"  slices  filet  mignon 

Saute  mushrooms  for  5  minutes  in  butter.   Add 
brandy  and  wines,  ignite,  let  flames  die  down 
Sprinkle  flour  over  mushrooms,  stir  in  sweet 
butter  till  melted.   Add  mustard.   Continue 
stirring  until  sauce  thickens.   Keep  warm 
over  low  heat.   Heat  iron  skillet  very  hot 
and  sprinkle  with  salt.   Pan  broil  filet 
slices,  4  minutes  on  first  side,  3  on  second 
(medium  rare).   Serve  filets  on  hot  plates 
and  spoon  sauce  over  them.   Serves  4. 

Kathy  Barnes

Black  Pepper  Steak 


IV  steak  (2  lbs.) 
Cracked  pepper 
1  Tablespoon  butter 
-2  cup  dry  white  wine 
Lump  of  butter 


Cover  both  sides  of  the  steak  very  generously 
with  cracked  pepper,  pressing  firmly  into  the 
meat.  In  an  iron  skillet,  over  a  high  flame, 
brown  both  sides  of  the  meat  in  butter.  Turn 
heat  down  and  cook  about  five  minutes  or  un- 
til done  enough.  Remove  to  hot  platter.  Stir 
wine  into  pan  juices  and  simmer  for  two 
minutes.  Add  lump  of  butter  and  pour, 
loose  pepper  and  all,  over  the  steak.  Serves 
4.

Cheeseburger  Pie 

1  lb .  ground  beef 

%  cup  evaporated  milk 

%  cup  catsup 

1/3  cup  dry  bread  crumbs 

H    cup  chopped  onion 

3/4  teaspoon  salt 

Sg  teaspoon  oregano 

1/8  teaspoon  pepper 

1  unbaked  pie  shell 

1  cup  shredded  cheese 

1  teaspoon  Worcestershire  sauce 

Dill  pickle  slices 

Thoroughly  combine  beef,  milk,  catsup,  crumbs, 
onion,  salt,  oregano  and  pepper.  Spread  in 
unbaked  pie  shell.  Bake  at  350°  for  35-40 
minutes.  Toss  together  the  cheese  and  Wor- 
cestershire. Spread  on  top  of  the  meat. 
Bake  10  minutes  more.  Remove  from  oven  and 
let  stand  10  minutes  before  serving.  Gar- 
nish with  dill  pickle  slices.  Serves  6.

Yorkshire  Pudding  (English) 

1  cup  white  flour 
Dash  salt 
1  egg 

1  cup  milk 

1  dessert  spoon  of  drippings  from 
roast  beef 

Sift  flour  into  bowl.  Make  a  nest  for  the 
egg  in  center  of  flour.  Add  about  half  of 
the  milk.  Stir  egg  and  milk  gradually, 
bringing  in  the  flour.  Add  milk  until  the 
amount  is  used  up.  Eeat.  Let  stand  half  an 
hour.  Heat  oven  to  425°.  Use  an  8"x8"  pan. 
Put  drippings  in  pan  and  put  into  oven  un- 
til fat  is  "smoking."  Pour  in  batter.  Cook 
for  10  minutes.  Reduce  heat  to  375°  for 
15-20  minutes.  Serve  with  the  roast  with 
gravy  or  butter.  Serves  4. 

Kay  Macdonald 

Yorkshire  Pudding  (American) 

1  cup  flour,  sifted  with  1  teaspoon  salt 
3  well  beaten  eggs 

2  cups  milk 

Drippings  in  roasting  pan 

Pour  off  drippings  from  roasting  pan, 
leaving  \    cup.  Combine  milk  and  eggs. 
Add  flour  and  salt  and  beat  well  in 
blender.  Pour  onto  hot  drippings  and 
bake  30  minutes  at  400°.

Fondue  Bourguignonne 

%  lb .  sirloin 

1  pint  salad  oil 

Cut  the  meat  in  slices  1"  thick  and  heap  on 
a  plate.  Just  before  eating,  heat  the  oil  on 
the  stove.  Fill  the  chafing  dish  a  little 
more  than  half  full  of  oil.  When  a  faint  haze 
rises  from  the  heating  oil,  transfer  it  to 
the  spirit  heater.  Each  guest  dips  his  meat, 
impaled  on  a  skewer  or  fork,  into  the  hot 
oil  until  cooked  to  his  taste.  While  the 
meat  is  cooking,  the  guests  serve  themselves 
to  the  sauces.  Remove  the  meat  from  the  cook- 
ing fork,  dip  it  into  a  sauce  and  eat. 

Gertrude  Marchetti

Stuffed  Cabbage  Rolls 


tedium  to  large  or 


1  cabbage  head, 

2  small  ones 
1  lb.  ground  meat  of  good  quality 
1  lb.  can  sauerkraut 
1  can  tomato  soup 
^  cup  rice,  cooked 
Salt,  pepper,  ketchup  and 

sauce  to  taste 


Worces  tershire 


Preboil  entire  cabbage  in  a  large  pot. 
Cut  leaves  individually,  one  at  a  time 
and  each  time  let  cabbage  cook  a  little 
longer.   Leaves  should  not  be  too  soft 
or  they  will  tear  but  they  must  be 
flexible.   Mix  hamburger,  rice  and  season- 
ings.  Fill  each  cabbage  leaf  with  this 
mixture  and  roll  it  firmly.   Wash  sauer- 
kraut several  times  and  mix  it  with  the 
tomato  soup.   On  the  bottom  of  a  large 
pot  or  casserole  place  a  few  leaves  that 
have  been  left  over,  a  layer  of  the  sauer 
kraut  mixture,  then  the  cabbage  rolls, 
closely  packed  one  to  another.   Top  the 
cabbage  rolls  with  remaining  sauerkraut 
mixture,  any  remaining  cabbage  leaves 
and  dot  with  butter.   Cook  for  1%  hours 
in  oven  375°-400°.   This  is  equally  good 
reheated.   Serves  4-6. 

Aleksandra  Gruzinska

Spaghetti  a  la  Rennolds 

2  quarts  canned  tomatoes 

4  cans  tomato  paste 

2  cans  tomato  soup 
1  Tablespoon  sugar 
1  Tablespoon  salt 

1  teaspoon  chili  powder 
1  teaspoon  cayenne 

3  cups  chopped  onions 

1  cup  finely  chopped  celery 

^  bunch  parsley 

6  lbs.  cheap  hamburger  or 

4  lbs .  ground  chuck 
1  green  pepper,  cut  in  half 
Olive  oil 
1  teaspoon  basil 
1  teaspoon  oregano  or  marjoram 

In  a  large  kettle  simmer  the  tomatoes,  break- 
ing them  up.   Add  tomato  paste,  soup  and 
seasonings.   Brown  onions  in  olive  oil  on 
fairly  low  heat.   When  golden  brown  add  them 
to  tomato  mixture.   Brown  celery  slightly  in 
same  pan,  adding  more  oil,  if  necessary.  Tear 
up  parsley  with  your  fingers  and  the  onion 
smell  will  disappear  from  your  hands.   Add 
celery  and  parsley  to  tomato  mixture.  Crumble 
beef  into  same  oniony  pan  and  brown  it.  Pour 
off  any  grease  and  add  meat  to  tomato  mixture 
Finally  wash  and  clean  green  pepper  and  drop 
it  into  mixture.   Simmer  for  4-6  hours,  stir- 
ring occasionally.   Remove  pepper  and  add 
basil  and  oregano.   Taste  for  salt.   Serves 
12. 

Seymour  L'aughon  Rennolds

Leg  of  Lamb 

5-6  lb.  leg  of  lamb 

Lemon,  salt,  pepper,  garlic  powder,  oregano 

Remove  mest  of  the  visible  fat  from  the 
lamb  and  rub  well  with  cut  lemon.   Sprinkle 
all  over  with  salt,  pepper  and  garlic  pow- 
der.  Sprinkle  with  oregano  and  rub  all 
over.   Bake  in  a  shallow  pan  in  oven  pre- 
heated to  400°,  for  15  minutes.   Reduce 
heat  to  325°  and  bake  until  meat  ther- 
mometer, inserted  in  meatiest  part  of  leg, 
reads  180°  or  slightly  more.   Remove  lamb 
from  pan  and  add  water  to  drippings  to  make 
gravy.

Very  Hot  Chili 

2  Tablespoons  bacon  drippings 
1  large  onion,  chopped 

1  lb .  ground  beef 

2  cups  canned  tomatoes 

4  cups  canned  chili  beans 

2  Tablespoons  chili  powder 

^  teaspoon  tabasco 

1  teaspoon  oregano 

\    teaspoon  Worcestershire 

^  teaspoon  garlic  salt 

h,    teaspoon  cayenne 

1  bay  leaf 

1  teaspoon  marjoram 

%  teaspoon  ground  cumin 

\    teaspoon  basil 

Saute  the  onion  in  drippings  for  a  few 
minutes.  Add  the  ground  beef  and  cook 
until  all  the  red  is  gone.  Add  the  rest

and  simmer  for  about  an  hour.  Uncover

rice .  Serves  6 .

Baked  Ham  Slice 


2  Tablespoons  brown  sugar 

1  cup  milk 

1  ham  slice,  cut  about  IV 


thick 


Melt  -sugar  in  a  heavy  skillet.  Add  ham  slice 
and  brown  on  both  sides.  Pour  milk  around  it 
and  bake  at  300°  for  30  minutes.  Remove  ham, 
thicken  gravy,  and  serve.  Serves  4-6. 


A  variation  calls  for  2  teaspoons  of  prepared 
mustard,  mixed  with  the  brown  sugar  and  rubbed 
over  the  ham  before  adding  milk.

Ham  in  Pastry 

4  cups  beef  stock 

1  cup  Port  wine 

1  carrot,  peeled  and  chopped 

1  medium  onion,  chopped 

5-6  lb.  canned  ham 

1  lb.  mushrooms,  chopped 
3  Tablespoons  butter 
Juice  of  %  lemon 

2  Tablespoons  instant  minced  onion 
2  green  onions,  chopped 

h.    teaspoon  each  salt,  thyme,  allspice 

Freshly  ground  pepper 

3-oz .  can  pate  de  f oie  gras 

h    cup  fine  bread  crumbs 

Pastry  (see  recipe) 

1  egg  yolk 

1  Tablespoon  water 

In  a  large  pan,  bring  to  a  boil  the  stock, 
wine,  carrot  and  onion.  Add  the  ham,  cover 
and  simmer  for  1  hour.  Remove  meat  from 
stock  and  drain.  Cool.  Reserve  stock.  Saute 
mushrooms  in  butter  and  sprinkle  with  lemon 
juice.  Add  instant  onion,  green  onion,  spices 
Remove  from  heat  and  stir  in  pate  and  bread 
crumbs.  Cool.  Roll  out  rich  pastry  about  3/8" 
thick  to  a  rectangle  about  14"xl8",  large 
enough  to  enclose  ham.  Save  scraps.  Spread 
the  mushroom  filling  over  the  pastry,  press- 
ing in  firmly  and  leaving  1%"  margin  on  all 
sides.  Place  meat,  top  side  down,  with  the 
long  side  of  ham  across  the  short  side  of 
pastry  center.  Wrap  pastry  around  the  meat 
and  seal  securely  down  the  middle  and  at  the 
ends,  moistening  pastry  edges  with  water. 
Place,  seam  side  down,  on  a  greased  baking 
sheet  and  garnish  with  designs  cut  from 
pastry  scraps.  Brush  pastry  with  mixture 
of  egg  yolk  beaten  with  1  Tablespoon  water. 
Bake  at  400°for  30  minutes.  Serve  hot  with 
reserved  stock.  Serves  12-14.

Rich  Pastry 

2h    cups  sifted  flour 

Jg  teaspoon  salt 

3/4  cup  butter 

3  egg  yolks,  beaten 

3-4  Tablespoons  cold  water 

Place  the  flour  and  salt  in  bowl.   Cut  in 
the  butter  until  particles  resemble  fine 
crumbs.   Mix  in  the  egg  yolks  and  water. 
Mix  lightly.   Press  into  a  ball,  cover  and 
chill.   Can  be  used  for  tarts,  and  for  Ham 
in  Crust.

h    cup  brown  sugar

8  3 


Country  Ham 

Soak  country  ham  for  about  24  hours.  Pour 
off  the  water.  Preheat  oven  to  500°.  Place 
ham  in  roaster  with  7  cups  of  water  and 
cover  tightly.  Place  in  oven  and  cook  15 
minutes.  Turn  off  the  heat.  DO  NOT  OPEN 
OVEN  DOOR.  Leave  for  3  hours.  Turn  heat 
on  to  375.  Cook  15  minutes.  Turn  off  heat. 
DO  NOT  OPEN  OVEN  DOOR.  Leave  over  night. 
Next  morning  skin  and  glaze  the  ham. 

Elizabeth  Bond  Wood 

Ham  and  Sauerkraut 

Slice  of  ham,  1"  thick 

2  apples,  peeled  and  cut  in  thin  slices 

\    teaspoon  celery  seed 

1  teaspoon  dry  mustard 

1/3  cup  molasses 

One  can  (303)  sauerkraut 

Place  sauerkraut  in  a  greased  shallow 
baking  dish  and  sprinkle  celery  seed 
over  it.  Cover  with  apple  slices.  Place 
ham  on  top.  Blend  mustard  and  molasses 
and  pour  over  ham.  Bake  at  350°  for  an 
hour  or  until  ham  and  apples  are  tender.

Meat  Balls  with  Spaghetti  Sauce 

2  lbs.  ground  beef 
2  large  eggs 
\    cup  parsley  flakes 
1  cup  grated  cheese  , 

1  large  onion,  chopped 
Salt ,  pepper 

2  large  cans  Italian  tomatoes 
1  can  Italian  tomato  paste 

3  cans  water 

Make  a  well  in  the  meat,  add  eggs,  parsley, 
cheese,  salt,  pepper.  Mix  with  fork,  then 
with  hands  until  mixture  leaves  bowl  clean. 
Form  into  small  meat  balls.  Brown  meat 
balls  in  skillet.  Brown  onions  in  same 
skillet  after  meat  balls  are  brown  on  one 
side  and  have  been  turned.  Onions  are  soft 
and  golden,  not  brown  by  time  meat  balls 
are  brown  on  other  side.  Remove  meat  balls. 
Cook  1  can  of  tomatoes  in  skillet  until  all 
meat  in  bottom  of  pan  becomes  mixed  with 
tomato.  Place  meat  balls,  sauce  from 
skillet,  tomato  paste,  water  and  remaining 
can  of  tomatoes  in  covered  pan.  Simmer  for 
at  least  2  hours.  Serves  6.

h    cup  brown  sugar 

Flour

Chinese  Red  Cooked  Pork  Shoulder 

1  3-6  lb.  pork  shoulder 

2  cups  water 
h    cup  sherry 

1  cup  soy  sauce 
4  slices  ginger 
4  green  onions 
1  Tablespoon  sugar 

Place  meat,  skin  side  up,  in  a  heavy  sauce- 
pan with  the  water.  Turn  heat  high  and  when 
water  boils,  pour  sherry  over  pork,  then  the 
soy  sauce.  Add  ginger  and  onions.  Cover  the 
pot,  lower  the  heat  and  simmer  for  one  hour. 
Turn  the  meat  and  simmer  another  hour.  Turn 
meat  again,  add  sugar  and  simmer  half  an  hour 
longer.  The  meat  should  be  tender  enough  to 
give  way  with  chopsticks.  Serve  in  a  deep 
bowl  with  the  gravy  poured  over  it.  Serves  6.

Spicy  Brisket 

8-12  lbs.  boneless  brisket 

1  box  crab  boil 

Salt 

Hickory  smoked  salt 

Chili  sauce 

Boil  meat  slowly  in  water  to  cover,  with 
salt  and  crab  boil,  for  2%  hours.  Let  meat 
cool  overnight  in  this  water.  Next  day 
place  brisket  on  a  foil  lined  cookie 
sheet.  Turn  up  edges  of  the  foil  to  form 
a  high  rim  around  the  meat,  leaving  a  large 
opening  at  the  top.  Sprinkle  top  with 
Hickory  salt,  cover  with  chili  sauce  and 
bake  about  an  hour  at  350°  till  the  meat 
is  hot  and  the  top  well  glazed.  Serves  8-12

Tongue  in  Sweet  and  Sour  Sauce 

4  gingersnaps 

h  cup  brown  sugar 

h  cup  vinegar 

1  cup  hot  water 

h  teaspoon  salt 

1  lemon,  sliced  paper  thin 

1  lb.  cooked  tongue,  sliced  thin 

Combine  ginersnaps,  sugar,  vinegar,  water, 
salt  and  lemon  in  a  saucepan  and  bring  to 
a  boil.   Lower  the  flame  and  let  simmer  10 
minutes.   When  the  consistency  is  as  thick 
as  you  want  it,  remove  from  heat  and  pour 
over  tongue.   This  can  be  made  a  few  days 
in  advance.   It  freezes  well.   Serves  6.

Sweet  Breads  Valhalla 

3  pairs  sweet  breads 
1  lemon 

1  onion,    sliced 

2  teaspoons    butter 

2  teaspoons  pickling  spice 

2  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

Flour 

H    teaspoon  dried  rosemary 

h    teaspoon  dried  basil 

1  bay  leaf 

H    teaspoon  seasoned  salt 

1  cup  brown  sauce 

H    teaspoon  Accent 

H    teaspoon  tarragon 

h    teaspoon  peppercorns 

h    teaspoon  salt 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

1  cup  sliced  mushrooms 

1  cup  chopped  green  onions 

h    cup  dry  sherry 

h    cup  beef  bouillon 

Soak  sweet  breads  2  hours  in  cold  water, 
salted.   Remove  and  put  in  pan.   Cover  with 
water  and  add  lemon,  onion,  bay  leaf,   pick- 
ling spices,  salt.   Bring  to  a  boil,  lower 
heat  and  simmer  15  minutes.   Put  sweet  breads 
in  cold  water  and  peel  off  membranes.   Heat 
butter  and  olive  oil  in  large  skillet.   Flour 
sweet  breads,  saute,  adding  rosemary,  basil, 
garlic,  peppercorns,  salt  and  seasoned  salt. 
Cook  until  golden  brown.   Add  mushrooms  and 
onions.   Continue  cooking  until  mushrooms 
and  onions  are  tender.   Add  sherry  and  beef 
bouillon.   Finally  add  1  cup  brown  sauce  or 
beef  gravy  and  cook  slowly  until  sweetbreads 
are  glazed,  about  6  minutes.   Serves  6. 

Beth  Gawthrop  T67

Vitello  Tonnato  (Veal  with  Tuna) 

1  5-lb .  leg  of  veal,  boned  and  rolled 

2  7-oz.  cans  of  tuna 

3  Tablespoons  oil 
2  garlic  cloves 

2  onions  coarsely  chopped 
2  celery  sticks,  cut  up 
h    cup  chopped  parsley 
2  bay  leaves 
\    teaspoon  thyme 
2  Tablespoons  salt 
Freshly  ground  pepper 
2  cups  chicken  stock 

1  2-oz.  can  flat  anchovy  fillets 
6  Tablespoons  lemon  juice 

2  cups  mayonnaise 

4  Tablespoons  capers 

1  lemon,  thinly  sliced 

Drain  the  oil  from  the  cans  of  tuna  fish  in- 
to a  Dutch  oven  or  large  pot  with  a  tight 
fitting  cover.  Add  the  3  Tablespoons  of  oil 
and  garlic  and  brown  the  veal  lightly.  Remove 
the  meat  and  set  it  aside.  Add  onions,  carrots 
and  celery  to  the  oil  and  cook,  stirring  fre- 
quently, for  5  minutes,  or  until  translucent. 
Add  parsley,  bay  leaves,  thyme,  salt,  pepper, 
chicken  stock,  tuna,  the  drained  anchovies  and 

2  Tablespoons  lemon  juice.  Stir  the  mixture 
well  to  dissolve  any  particles  that  may  stick 
to  the  bottom  of  the  pot.  Bri'ng  to  a  boil, 
then  add  the  veal.  Reduce  heat,  cover  and 
simmer  for  3  hours.  Remove  the  veal  from  the 
pot  and  cool  to  room  temperature.  Chill  in 
the  refrigerator.  Meanwhile  put  the  pot  back 
on  the  stove  and  reduce  the  vegetable-tuna 
mixture  (about  5-6  cups)  to  about  4  cups, 
stirring  from  time  to  time.  Puree  the 
vegetable-tuna  mixture  in  a  blender  or  put 

it  through  a  food  mill.  Add  2  cups  of 


92 


the  puree  to  2  cups  of  mayonnaise  along  with 
4  Tablespoons  of  lemon  juice  and  2  Tablespoons 
of  capers.  Refrigerate.  Before  serving  slice 
the  veal  in  thin  slices  and  arrange  them  on  a 
large  platter.  Spoon  half  the  tuna-mayonnaise 
over  veal  slices,  garnish  with  lemon  slices 
and  rest  of  capers.  Pass  remaining  sauce. 

Ruth  Clarkson  Costello

Veal  Cutlets  Parmesan

h    teaspoon  parsley 

h    teaspoon  oregano

3  Tablespoons  butter

H    lb.  Mozzarello  cheese 

\    cup  freshly  grated  Parmesan

Flatten  cutlets  with  meat  hammer  until  about 
1/8"  thick.   Cut  into  serving  pieces  and 
sprinkle  lightly  with  sage.   Beat  eggs  well, 
adding  cream,  salt  and  pepper.   Mix  bread 
crumbs,  parsley  and  oregano.   Dip  cutlets 
in  egg  mixture  and  then  bread  crumb  mixture.

greased  pan,  8lfxl2"xlVf  .   Cover  with  tomato 
sauce  and  place  a  thin  slice  of  Mozzarello. 
cheese  over  each  cutlet.   Bake  at  375°  for

oven,  sprinkle  with  Parmesan  cheese  and 
serve  hot.   Serves  4.

Chicken  in  Cream 

8  pieces  of  chicken,  b roile r- f rye r 

3  Tablespoons  butter  (not  margarine) 

2  cups  thinly  sliced  yellow  onions 

^  teaspoon  salt 

1/8  teaspoon  white  pepper 

hi    teaspoon  curry  powder 

^  cup  dry  white  wine 

2\    cups  whipping  cream 

Salt  and  pepper  to  taste 

%    cup  whipping  cream 

Fresh  parsley 

Melt  butter  in  heavy  10"  skillet  or  electric* 
fry  pan  over  medium  heat.  Dry  chicken  pieces 
well  and  place  in  butter  for  4-5  minutes.  Do 
not  brown.  Remove  chicken  to  side  dish.  Stir 
onions  into  skillet  over  low  heat.  Cover  and 
cook  slowly  5  minutes.  Do  not  brown.  Return 
chicken  to  skillet  with  onions  and  cook  slowly 
8  minutes.  Do  not  brown.  Turn  once  only.  Add 
salt,  pepper,  curry  powder  and  wine  to  chicken 
Turn  up  heat  and  boil  till  most  of  liquid 
evaporates.  As  liquid  evaporates,  place  2h 
cups  of  whipping  cream  in  a  small  saucepan. 
Bring  cream  to  a  slow  boil.  Pour  hot  cream 
into  skillet  and  simmer  gently  25-30  minutes. 
Remove  chicken  to  platter  to  keep  warm.  At 
this  point,  cooking  may  be  stopped  until 
serving  time  (2-3  hours  at  most).  10  minutes 
before^  serving,  skim  fat  off  sauce  in  skillet. 
Boil  rapidly,  stirring  until  sauce  reduces, 
thickens  and  will  coat  a  spoon.  Add  few  drops 
of  lemon  juice  to  taste  and  more  salt  and 
pepper,  if  needed.  Smooth  out  sauce  with  rest 
of  whipping  cream.  Place  chicken  in  serving 
dish  or  use  platter  which  has  been  kept  warm. 
Pour  sauce  over  chicken.  Garnish  with  parsley. 

Bill  Knight

Olive  oil

%  lb.  almonds,  blanched  and  browned  lightly

put  in  casserole.   Add  the  onion,  pepper

Chicken  Kiev 

4  chicken  breasts,  skinned,  boned,  halved 

and  pounded  flat 
%  lb.  butter  or  margarine 
2  Tablespoons  chopped  parsley 
%  teaspoon  salt 
^  teaspoon  white  pepper 
Flour 

1  egg,  beaten 
Dry  bread  crumbs 

Mix  seasonings  with  butter  and  divide  into 
8  lumps  or  balls.  Place  a  seasoned  ball  in 
the  center  of  each  half  chicken  breast  and 
roll,  enveloping  butter  completely.  Secure 
with  toothpick.  Dust  with  flour,  brush  with 
beaten  egg  and  roll  in  crumbs.  Fry  in  deep 
fat  5-7  minutes  till  golden  brown. 

(A  favorite  of  Anne  Pannell  Taylor  at 
Sweet  Briar  House.) 


It  is  possible  to  keep  parsley  and  water- 
cress fresh  for  days.  Wash  and  let  drain. 
Place  loosely  in  quart  mason  jar  and  screw 
on  the  cap.  Invert  in  refrigerator. 


You  Qan  freeze  mint  leaves,  parsley  and 
chives  for  winter  use.  Wash  well,  shake 
dry  and  freeze  in  plastic  containers. 
They  will  not  be  crisp  but  the  flavor 
will  be  good .

Oven  Barbecued  Chicken 

2  broilers,  quartered 

1  large  onion,  sliced 

2/3  cup  catsup 

1/3  cup  vinegar 

4  Tablespoons  butter 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

1  teaspoon  rosemary,  crushed 

1  teaspoon  salt 

h    teaspoon  dry  mustard 

Place  chicken,  skin  side  down  in  a  shallow 
buttered  baking  pan.  Top  with  onion  slices 
Mix  remaining  ingredients  in  a  small  pan 
and  heat  to  boiling.  Pour  over  chicken. 
Bake  at  400°  for  30  minutes,  turn  chicken, 
baste  with  sauce.  Continue  baking  and 
basting,  for  30  minutes  longer.  Serves  8. 

Edna  Armstrong

To  brown  chicken  or  lean  meats

Hot  Chicken  Loaf 


cups  coarsely  ground,  cooked  chicken 

cup  bread  crumbs 

can  cream  chicken  soup 

cup  celery,  chopped 

cup  onion,  chopped 

slightly  beaten  eggs 

teaspoon  seasoned  salt 
1  Tablespoon  parsley 
1  can  mushroom  soup 


Mix  the  chicken  soup  into  the  beaten  eggs 
and  lightly  combine  with  celery,  onion, 
chicken,  crumbs  and  seasoning.  Line  a 
greased  loaf  pan  with  foil,  grease  the 
foil.  Turn  in  the  chicken  mixture  and  bake 
at  350°  for  45  minutes,  or  until  center  is 
firm.  Invert  onto  serving  platter  and  re- 
move foil.  Serve  with  mushroom  sauce,  made 
by  heating  the  undiluted  mushroom  soup. 
Serves  6 . 

Mary  Ann  Lee 

Oven-fried  Chicken  in  Cheese  Crumbs 

6  chicken  breasts  or  legs 

Salad  oil 

1  cup  crumbs  made  from  cheese  crackers 

Dip  chicken  in  salad  oil  and  roll  in 
crumbs.  Arrange  on  greased  cookie  sheet 
and  bake  one  hour  at  350°.  Serves  6. 

Carolyn  Bates

King  Ranch  Chicken 

12  tortillas 

3  lbs.  boiled,  boned  chicken 

1  can  #2  tomatoes  with  juice 

1  can  cream  mushroom  soup 

2  Tablespoons  chopped  onion 

1  4-oz  .  can  chopped  mushrooms,  drained 

2  Tablespoons  Old  El  Paso  chile  and  tomato 

mixture  or  jalepeno  relish 
1  cup  grated  cheddar  cheese 

Line  a  3  quart  casserole  with  one  half  of 
the  tortillas  and  on  top  make  a  layer  of 
h    of  each  ingredient  listed,  in  the  order 
listed,  with  the  exception  of  the  cheese. 
Put  the  whole  cup  of  cheese  on  the  top  of 
a  second  layer,  made  from  the  other  half  of 
the  ingredients.  Bake  in  a  350°  oven  for  50 
minutes.  Turn  off  oven  and  let  casserole  set 
for  30  minutes.  Serve.  Serves  8. 

E.Lind  Dore  Deay 

Parmesan  Fried  Chicken 


1  cup  packaged  herb  stuffing,   crushed 
2/3  cup  grated  Parmesan  cheese 
h    cup  chopped  parsley 
1  clove  garlic,  crushed 


cup  butter,  melted 


lb 


fryer,  disjointed 


Combine  crumbs,  cheese,  parsley  and  garlic. 
Dip  chicken  in  butter,  then  in  crumbs.  Place 
pieces,  skin  side  up,  in  shallow  pan  lined 
with  foil.  Bake  in  oven  at  350°  for  one  hour 
or  till  tender.  Serves  6.

Chicken  Nicoise 

4  broilers,  halved 

Lemon  juice 

4  Tablespoons  butter,  melted 

2  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

Salt  and  pepper 

White  wine 

2  large  onions,  chopped 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
1  cup  chicken  stock 

%  cup  pitted  halved  ripe  olives 

1  cup  tomato  puree 

3  bay  leaves 

%    teaspoon  each  saffron,  oregano,  marjoram, 

rosemary,  thyme,  tarragon 
^  teaspoon  each  basil,  celery  seed,  pepper, 

fennel 
3/4  cup  white  wine 
H    cup  pimiento,  chopped 

2  cloves  garlic,  crushed 

Rub  broilers  with  lemon  juice,  inside  and  out 
Brush  with  butter  and  olive  oil.   Dust  with 
salt  and  pepper  and  roast  at  300°  about  40 
minutes  till  a  delicate  brown  and  barely  ten- 
der.  Cool.   Set  aside.   Scrape  all  juices 
from  roasting  pan,  adding  a  little  wine,  and 
boiling  till  pan  can  be  scraped  clean.   Add 
onions,  fry  in  butter  till  limp.   Add  chicken 
stock,  pur^e,  bay  leaves,  spices,  wine, 
pimiento,  garlic,  and  olives.   Simmer  for  15 
minutes.   An  hour  before  dinner,  arrange 
chickens  in  roaster,  cut  side  down.   Pour 
the  sauce  over  them.   Cover  and  bake  at  350° 
for  45  minutes.   Remove  cover  and  bake  for 
15  minutes.   Serves  8. 

Elizabeth  Sprague

World's  Fair  Chicken 

3  broilers,  halved 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
Salt  and  pepper 

lh    cups  orange  juice 

h    cup  raisins 

h    cup  chopped  chutney 

%    cup  slivered  almonds 

^  teaspoon  cinnamon 

h    teaspoon  curry  powder 

Dash  of  thyme 

Hot  cooked  rice 

3  bananas,  sliced 

1  small  can  mandarin  oranges 
1  cup  each:  green  onion,  bacon,  coconut 
chips,  parsley  sprigs 

Arrange  chicken  halves  in  greased  shallow 
baking  dish.   Dot  with  butter.   Sprinkle 
with  salt  and  pepper.   Bake  at  425°  for  15 
minutes.   Meanwhile,  in  a  saucepan,  combine 
orange  juice,  raisins,  chutney,  almonds, 
cinnamon,  curry  and  thyme.   Pour  sauce  over 
browned  chicken.   Bake  at  350°  for  1  hour 
or  until  chicken  is  tender.   To  serve 
arrange  chicken  on  bed  of  hot  rice. 
Garnish  with  banana  slices  and  orange 
sections.   Accompany  with  condiments, 
parsley.   6  servings.

Curried  Date  Chicken 


2^-3  lbs.  broiler-fryer  chickens,  cut 

1  cup  flour 

2  teaspoons  salt 

1  teaspoon  garlic  salt 

\    teaspoon  pepper 

3h    Tablespoons  butter  or  oleo 

3  medium  onions,  sliced 

1  Tablespoon  curry  powder 

2  cups  water 

\    cup  chopped  dates 

\    cup  parsley,  cut  fine 


up 


Shake  chicken  pieces  in  a  bag  containing 
flour,  salt,  garlic  salt  and  pepper.  In  a 
large  skillet  brown  chicken  well  in  butter. 
Remove.  Add  onions  and  saute  till  trans- 
parent. Stir  in  curry.  Add  chicken  and 
water.  Simmer  covered  till  chicken  is 
done  -  40-50  minutes.  Stir  in  dates  and 
sprinkle  with  parsley.  Serve  with  rice. 
Serves  4 . 

Denise  Limouze 

Curried  Chicken 

For  curried  chicken  in  a  hurry  open  one  or 
more  cans  of  chicken  fricassee,  season  to 
taste  with  curry  powder,  onion  juice,  lemon 
juice  and  thyme.  Heat  and  serve  with  rice 
and  chutney.

Poulet  Jardiniere 

h,    cup  buttery  Wesson  oil 
3/4  cup  chicken  broth 
3/4  cup  cooking  sherry 

1  package  frozen  artichokes 

2  tomatoes,  cut  in  wedges 

1  onion,  sliced 

h    green  pepper,  sliced 
Salt,  pepper,  paprika 
Flour 

3  lb.  frying  chicken 

Preheat  electric  skillet  to  350°.   Dredge 
chicken  in  flour  and  seasonings.   Brown 
slowly  in  hot  fat.   Reduce  temperature  to 
250°.   Add  chicken  broth  and  sherry.  Cover. 
Cook  45  minutes.   Sprinkle  vegetables  with 
salt,  add  them  and  continue  cooking  till 
artichokes  are  done,  about  15  minutes. 
Serves  4. 

Denise  Limouze 

Count  Me  In  Chicken 

2  chicken    breasts,    halved 

4  pieces    of    bacon 

4  large  pieces  of  chipped  beef 
1  can  cream  of  mushroom  soup 
1  cup  sour  cream 

Debone  the  chicken.   Wrap  each  piece  in  a 
slice  of  bacon.   Next  wrap  each  piece  in  a 
thin  layer  of  chipped  beef.   Place  chicken 
pieces  in  an  ungreased  baking  dish,  about 
8x8x4".   Mix  the  soup  and  sour  cream.   Pour 
over  the  chicken  and  bake  uncovered  at  325° 
for  3  hours.   Serves  4. 

Frances  Arthur,  R.N.

Deviled  Chicken  with  Oyster  Sauce 


2  fryers,  quartered 

2  Tablespoons  dry  mustard 

4  teaspoons  cold  water 

1  cup  cracker  crumbs 

1  teaspoon  salt 

^  cup  butter 

Paprika 

18  oysters 

h    cup  butter,  melted 

1  medium  onion,  chopped 
h  clove  garlic,  crushed 
Jg  cup  flour 

%    cup  milk 

lh    cups  chicken  stock 

2  Tablespoons  chili  sauce 
2  teaspoons  sugar 

2  teaspoons  prepared  mustard 

lh    teaspoons  each  ginger,  salt,  mustard 

h    teaspoon  paprika 

Cayenne 

1  Tablespoon  lemon  juice 

Parsley 

Remove  skin  from  the  chicken  with  paper  towel 
Mix  together  mustard,  water  to  make  a  paste. 
Spread  on  chicken  and  roll  in  crumbs  mixed 
with  salt.  Saute  in  butter  until  brown.  Re- 
move chicken  from  pan  and  drain.  Place  in 
2h    quart  casserole  and  cover  tightly.  Cook 
for  1  hour  at  350°.  Drain  any  liquid  from 
casserole,  sprinkle  with  paprika.  Add  lemon 
juice  to  oyster  sauce,  pour  over  chicken  and 
garnish  with  parsley. 


108 


Oy s  t er  Sauce 

Drain  oysters  as  dry  as  possible.  Melt  but- 
ter in  saucepan  and  add  onion  and  garlic. 
Cook,  stirring  constantly,  until  onion  is 
transparent..  Add  flour,  milk  and  stock. 
Cook  until  thick.  Season  with  chili  sauce, 
sugar,  mustard,  and  spices.  Simmer  20  minutes, 
stirring  occasionally.  Cut  oysters  in  small 
pieces  and  add  to  sauce.  Cook  3  minutes 
longer.  Keep  hot  over  low  heat  until  ready 
to  serve.  Serves  8. 

Marjorie  Jordan 

Barbeque  Sauce  for  Chicken 


cup  salad  oil 

large  onion,  finely  chopped 

Tablespoon  catsup 


1  teaspoon  A-l  sauce 
Salt  and  Pepper  to  taste 

Combine  all  ingredients  in  saucepan  and 
heat  until  boiling.  Stir  and  lower  heat 
or  keep  at  edge  of  grill.  After  chickens 
have  been  seared  on  both  sides  over  hot 
fire,  elevate  them  and  baste  with  sauce. 
Continue  cooking  and  basting  for  at  least 
an  hour .

Chinese  Walnut  Chicken 


1  cup  broken  walnuts 
%  cup  salad  oil 

2  raw  chicken  breasts,  cut  in  thin  strips 
%  teaspoon  salt 

1  cup  onion  slices 

1%    cups  bias  cut  celery 

lh    cups  chicken  broth 

1  teaspoon  sugar 

1  Tablespoon  cornstarch 

cup  soy  sauce 

Tablespoons  sherry 

5-oz.  can  bamboo  shoots 

5-oz.  can  water  chestnuts,  sliced 


Toast  walnuts  in  hot  oil,  drain  on  paper 
towel.  Put  chicken  in  skillet,  sprinkle 
with  salt,  cook  5  to  10  minutes,  stirring 
frequently.  Remove  from  pan.  Put  onions, 
celery,  h    cup  chicken  broth  in  skillet. 
Cook  5  minutes.  Combine  sugar,  cornstarch, 
soy  sauce,  sherry  and  remaining  chicken 
broth.  Pour  over-  vegetables  in  skillet. 
Cook  and  stir  until  sauce  thickens.  Add 
chicken,  bamboo  shoots  and  water  chestnuts 
Heat  through.  Serve  over  rice.  Serves  6. 


Quick  Chicken  Paprika 

Brown  a  sliced  onion  in  butter.  Add  1  Table- 
spoon paprika  and  4  Tablespoons  water  and 
simmer  till  onions  are  tender.  Add  to  1  can 
chicken  fricassee  the  onions  and  h    teaspoon 
tarragon.  Heat  thoroughly  but  do  not  boil. 
Add  h    cup  sour  cream.  Do  not  mix,  just  streak 
it  into  chicken  mixture.  Serve  on  rice  with 
shredded  almonds  on  top.

Chicken  Livers  with  Burgundy 

2  lbs.  chicken  livers 
^  cup  butter 

3  medium  tomatoes,  chopped 
Ground  pepper 

^  cup  Burgundy 
3/4  teaspoon  salt 
1  teaspoon  Rosemary 

Rinse  and  dry  livers.   Cut  each  piece  on 
the  edge  to  keep  from  curling  during  cook- 
ing.  Melt  butter  in  skillet  and  when 
sizzling,  add  livers.   Brown  quickly.   Add 
tomatoes,  wine  and  seasonings.   Reduce 
heat  and  cook  5-8  minutes.   Serve  over 
rice  or  toast.   Serves  4.

Salt

112 


Roast  Duck  with  Orange 

1  duck 

2  apples,  cut  in  thin  slices 

4  oranges,  2  sliced,  2  for  juice 

2  cloves 

1  jigger  each  cointreau,  curacao,  cognac 

4  bouillon  cubes 

1  cup  boiling  water 

1  teaspoon  cornstarch 
Margarine 

Stuff  duck  with  apples,  orange  slices,  cloves, 
curacao.   Sew  up.   Braise  duck  in  margarine, 
flambez  with  cognac.   Pour  over  it  juice  of 
one  orange  and  bouillon  cubes  melted  in  boil- 
ing water.   Cover  and  cook  one  hour  at  350°. 
Cut  up  orange  peel  in  small  pieces  and  boil 
2-3  minutes  to  get  rid  of  oil.   Drain  and 
mix  with  cornstarch  and  cointreau.   Add  to 
gravy.   Remove  duck  from  gravy  and  brown. 
Finally  return  to  gravy  and  add  juice  of 
4th  orange.   Serves  4. 

Kathy  Barnes 

Rock  Cornish  Game  Hen 

6  small  game  hens,  cleaned 
6  Tablespoons  butter 

3  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

2  cups  dry  white  wine 
Salt 

Pepper 

6  shallots,  chopped 

2  cups  button  mushrooms 

Heat  oil  and  butter  in  heavy  pan.  Brown  hens 
lightly  and  evenly.  Add  wine  and  seasonings, 
cover  and  cook  20  minutes,  or  until  tender. 
Add  shallots  and  mushrooms  and  cook  20  minutes 
longer.  Pour  pan  sauce  over  hens  and  serve 
with  wild  rice.   Serves  6.
