Paella  a  la  Valenciana 


18  pieces  frying  chicken 

Olive  oil 

2  cloves  garlic,  crushed 


medium  onions,  chopped 


green  pepper,  chopped 
teaspoon  saffron 
cup  cooked  pork  or  ham, 
teaspoons  paprika 
teaspoon  Oregano 
3/4  cup  parsley,  chopped 
cup  green  onion,  chopped 
cups  raw  rice 
cup  minced  clams 
lb.  peeled  shrimp 
raw  tomatoes,  chopped 
cups  chicken  stock 


diced 


Brown  chicken  in  oil.  Remove  from  pan  and 
saute  onion  and  pepper.  Add  chicken  stock 
and  garlic.  Add  saffron,  paprika,  Oregano, 
parsley  and  green  onion.  Next  add  shrimp, 
clams  and  heat  well.  Season  with  salt  and 
pepper,  add  tomatoes,  and  rice.  Stir  well. 
Place  chicken  pieces  on  top  of  rice,  then 
pork  or  ham.  Cook,  uncovered,  in  a  large, 
flat  pan  for  45  minutes  at  400°.  Do  not 
stir.  Se  rves  18 . 

Lucy  Lombardi

Oven  Baked  Chicken 

2-2%  lb.  chicken,  quartered 
Melted  butter 
Salt 
Pepper 

8  Tablespoons  sherry- 
Rice  Crispies 
%  cup  mushrooms 
1  Tablespoon  flour 
1  cup  milk 

Brush  chicken  with-  butter.  Sprinkle 
salt  and  pepper  over  chicken.  Put  1 
Tablespoon  sherry  on  each  piece  of 
chicken,  then  sprinkle  with  crushed 
Rice  Crispies.  Bake  at  350°  until  ten- 
der, about  1  hour.  Baste  often.  Add 
water  to  pan  if  it  gets  too  dry.  Re- 
move chicken  from  the  pan.  Saute  mush- 
rooms  in  the  drippings,  add  minced 
liver  and  gizzard  which  have  already 
been  cooked,  1  Tablespoon  flour  and 
milk.  If  necessary  to  thin,  add  half- 
and-half.  Serves  8. 

Alma  Thomas

Poulet  Provencal 

8  chicken  thighs 
8  strips  of  bacon 
1  cup  chopped  onion 

1  cup  chopped  tomato 

2  cloves  crushed  garlic 

3  oz.  cream  cheese 

4  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

4  crushed  juniper  berries 
White  wine 
Paprika,  Salt 

Wrap  each  thigh  with  a  strip  of  bacon. 
Dip  in  flour,  sprinkle  with  paprika  and 
salt  and  fry  in  olive  oil.  In  a  casserole 
simmer  onion,  tomato,  garlic,  juniper 
berries  and  olive  oil.  Season  with  salt 
to  taste.  Place  browned  chicken  on  top 
of  tomato-onion  mixture,  cover  with  white 
wine  and  cook  in  covered  casserole  for  45 
minutes  at  350°.  Remove  chicken  and  keep 
warm.  Stir  cream  cheese  into  liquid, 
bring  to  boil  and  pour  over  chicken. 
Serve  with  rice.  Serves  4. 

Sandra  Horwege

Crab  Timbale 


2  cups  medium  white  sauce 

2  hard  cooked  eggs,  sliced 

1  3-oz.  can  mushrooms 

6  large  stuffed  olives 

6%  oz .  can  crab 

1-2  Tablespoons  sherry 

Dash  tabasco 

Dash  Worcestershire 

Salt 

Pepper 


Combine  all  ingredients,  heat  and  serve  in 
timbale  shells,  on  toast  or  rusk,  or  in 
patty  shells.  Serves  6. 

Crabmeat  Salad  Cups 


package  patty  shells,  cooked 

cup  crabmeat,  flaked 

cups  bias-cut  celery

cup  ripe  olives,  sliced

onions.  Combine  mayonnaise,  sour  cream,  wine

Bake  at  350°  for  25  minutes  or  until  bubbly.

%  cup  bread  crumbs

Fast  Fish  Chowder 

1  lb.  fish  fillets,  thawed,  cut  into 

2"  squares 

2  cans  frozen  cream  potato  soup 
2  soup-cans  milk 

1  bay  leaf 

2  teaspoons  freeze-dried  chives 

Bring  the  soup,  milk  and  herbs  to  a  boil, 
stirring  occasionally.  Add  fish.  Bring  to 
a  boil  and  simmer  10  minutes,  or  until 
fish  flakes  easily.  Garnish  each  serving 
with  parsley  or  bacon  bits.  Makes  about 
1H    quarts.  Serves  6.

Baked  Seafood 

1  lb.  of  halibut

crab,  thawed  (6  to  6h    oz.  each)

h    cup  cream

Pinch  of  pepper

Paprika

cup  butter 


h    cup  lemon  juice

h    cup  light  cream

Coquilles  Saint  Jacques 

1  lb.  scallops,  washed 
%  lb.  mushrooms,  sliced 

1  cup  dry  white  wine  or  3/4  cup  dry 

white  vermouth 

2  teaspoons  green  onions  or  shallots, 

minced 

1  piece  of  a  bay  leaf 
Sprig^of  parsley 
Pinch  of  thyme 

\    teaspoon  salt 

Sauce : 

3  Tablespoons  butter 
3  Tablespoons  flour 

2  egg  yolks,  beaten  slightly 
Jg  cup  whipping  cream 

1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 
%  cup  milk 

Put  scallops,  mushrooms,  onions  and  season- 
ings in  a  saucepan,  add  wine  and  water  enough 
to  cover.  Simmer,  covered  for  5  minutes.  Re- 
move scallops  and  mushrooms  with  slotted  spoon 
and  set  aside.  Boil  down  liquid  until  it  is  re 
duced  to  a  cup.  Mal^e  a  cream  sauce  of  butter, 
flour,  milk  and  liquid.  Cook  one  minute.  Com- 
bine egg  yolks  and  cream  and  beat  hot  sauce 
into  them  very  gradually.  Cook  one  minute. 
Add  lemon  juice.  Cut  scallops  into  small 
pieces  and  add  them  with  mushrooms  to  the 
sauce:  Put  in  buttered  shells.  Cover  with 
bread  crumbs  and  dot  with  butter.  Place 
under  broiler  for  3-4  minutes  until  brown.

Shrimp  Curry 

1  teaspoon  curry  powder 
h    cup  Chopped  onions 

2  Tablespoons  butter 

1  can  frozen  shrimp  soup 

1  cup  sour  cream 

1  lb.  cooked  shrimp

hot,  fluffy  rice.   Serves  6.

Shrimp 

lh    lbs .  shrimp 

1  Tablespoon  vinegar 

3  Tablespoons  onions,  chopped 

4-5  Tablespoons  olive  oil 

h    cup  white  wine 

1  cup  tomato  sauce 

Salt  and  pepper 

1  bay  leaf 

1  teaspoon  sugar 

1  teaspoon  cornstarch 

2  Tablespoons  parsley,  chopped 
1  Tablespoon  butter 

Boil  shrimp  in  salted  water  with  vinegar 
for  15  or  20  minutes.   When  cool,  shell 
and  devein.   Cook  onions  in  olive  oil  un- 
til transparent.   Add  wine,  tomato  sauce, 
salt  and  pepper  to  taste,  bay  leaf  and 
sugar.   Simmer  uncovered  for  25-30  minutes. 
Mix  cornstarch  with  a  little  water  and  add 
it  to  the  sauce  stirring  constantly.   Cook 
till  it  boils.   Add  parsley  and  butter.   Add 
shrimp.   Cook  for  a  few  minutes  longer  and 
serve  hot  over  Pilaf.   Serves  6. 

Penny  Lagakos 


Leftover  shrimp,  minced  and  mixed  with  chopped 
cucumber  and  onion  juice  or  chives  and  seasoned 
with  mayonnaise  and  French  dressing  will  make 
good  sandwich  filling  or  stuffing  for  small 
rolls  .

Tuna  and  Shrimp  Curry 

1%    cups  chopped  onions 
4  Tablespoons  butter 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

3  Tablespoons  curry  powder 

2  Tablespoons  flour 
1  teaspoon  salt 

1  1/3  cups  milk 

1  can  frozen  shrimp  soup,  thawed 

2  cans  chunk-style  tuna 
2  cups  cooked  shrimp 

2  cups  sour  cream 

Saute  the  onions  and  garlic  in  the  butter, 
in  a  large  skillet.   Add  curry  powder  and 
flour  and  cook  for  2  minutes.   Add  milk, 
stirring  constantly  and  cook  till  thick. 
Add  the  soup,  tuna,  and  shrimp*.   Heat 
thoroughly.   Add  sour  cream  and  heat  but 
DO  NOT  BOIL.   Serve  over  Rice  and  Raisins. 
Serves  8. 

*You  may  substitute  4  cups  of  seafood. 

Ann  Aiken

1/3  cup  finely  grated  sharp  cheddar  cheese 
and  paprika.

Apple-Filled  Squash 

3  acorn  squash 

2  Tablespoons  butter,  melted 

1  lb.  2  oz .  can  pie  sliced  apples 

1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 

h    teaspoon  powdered  ginger 

3  Tablespoons  butter 
3/4  cup  brown  sugar 

Halve  squash  lengthwise.  Remove  seeds. 
Brush  with  melted  butter  and  sprinkle 
with  a  little  salt.  Place,  cut  side  down, 
in  large  baking  dish.  Bake  at  350°  for  35 
minutes.  Combine  apples,  brown  sugar, 
lemon  juice  and  ginger.  Turn  squash,  cut 
side  up,  in  baking  dish.  Fill  centers  with 
apple  mixture.  Dot  with  butter.  Continue 
baking  25  minutes  more,  till  squash  is 
tender.  If  desired,  sprinkle  with  ground 
cinnamon  before  serving.  Serves  6. 

Celery,  cut  into  fine  diagonal  pieces,  is 
good  cooked  with  peas  or  beans.

Red  Cabbage  with  Chestnuts 

1  medium  head  red  cabbage 
4  Tablespoons  butter 

1  medium  onion,  sliced 

3  celery  stalks,  chopped 

2  tart  apples,  peeled,  cut 
1  green  pepper,  chopped 
1/3  cup  wine  vinegar 

h    cup  Port  wine 

3  oz.  jar  currant  jelly 
1  teaspoon  cumin 

1  cup  cooked  chestnuts 

Shred,  wash  and  drain  the  cabbage.   In  a 
saucepan  melt  the  butter;  saute  the  onion, 
celery,  apples,  green  pepper  till  limp.  Add 
the  well  drained  cabbage.   Stir  and  cover 
and  cook  for  20  minutes  over  a  low  flame. 
Add  vinegar,  wine,  jelly  and  cumin.   Stir 
till  blended.   Cover.   Simmer  15  minutes . 
Add  chestnuts.   Simmer  10  minutes.   Salt 
and  pepper  to  taste  and  serve  hot.   Serves 
6.

through.  Serves  6.

drained,  mashed  together  and  seasoned  with 
cream,  salt  and  papper  make  a  good  winter 
vegetable  dish.

Halune 

4  pounds  asparagus 

4  onions,  chopped 

V%    cups  olive  oil 

H    teaspoon  salt 

3/4  teaspoon  ground  pepper 

4  cups  boiling  water 

Juice  of  two  lemons,  strained 

Cut  the  asparagus  in  2"  pieces.   Saute 
the  onions  in  the  oil  in  a  4-quart  kettle 
until  golden  brown.   Add  asparagus,  salt, 
pepper,  boiling  water  and  cook  uncovered 
15  minutes  or  until  tender.   Sprinkle 
lemon  juice  over  asparagus  and  serve  hot. 
Serves  6. 

Patty  Lynas  Ford

Vegetable  Tricks 

Rice  Amandine  -  Cook  2  cups  rice,  add 
4  Tablespoons  butter,  salt  to  taste 
"H.    pound  blanched  and  fried  almonds. 


String  be'ans  Indiana  -  Add  crumbled  cooked 
bacon  and  chopped  raw  onion  before  serv- 
ing. 

Artichoke  hearts  -  Melt  and  blend  in  the 
top  of  a  double  boiler,  1  stick  butter 
and  1  small  wedge  of  blue  cheese. 
Drain  two  cans  of  artichoke  hearts, 
cut  in  halves  or  quarters  and  heat  in 
the  butter-cheese  sauce. 

Summer  squash  with  chives  -  Add  cut  up  chives 
to  summer  squash  before  serving.  They  add 
color  and  zip .

Calico  Rice  Bake 

3/4  cup  water 

1  Tablespoon  instant  onion 
3/4  teaspoon  salt 

Dash  pepper 

Dash  crushed  rosemary 

2  cups  Minute  Rice 

1  cup  shredded  cheese 
2/3  cup  evaporated  milk 

3  beaten  eggs 

2  cups  mixed  vegetables,  drained 

In  medium  saucepan  combine  water,  onion, 
salt,  pepper  and  rosemary.  Bring  just  to 
boil.  Stir  in  rice.  Cover  tightly;  remove 
from  heat  and  let  stand  5  minutes.  Fluff 
with  a  fork.  Stir  in  cheese,  milk  and 
eggs.  Add  vegetables.  Turn  into  shallow 
baking  dish.  Bake,  uncovered,  at  350 
for  25  minutes,  or  till  inserted  knife 
comes  out  clean.  Serves  6. 

Corn  Pudding 

1  can  cream-style  corn 

2  egg  yolks 
1  cup  milk 

H    teaspoon  salt 

Dash  cayenne 

h    Tablespoon  melted  butter 

Combine  the  ingredients,  put  in  a  shallow 
casserole  and  set  in  a  pan  of  hot  water. 
Bake  at  350°  for  45  minutes  to  1  hour. 
Serves  6 . 

Lydia  Newland

Baked  Rice 

1  cup  rice 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

1  small  onion,  chopped 

1  cup  tomato  juice 

1  cup  beef  bouillon 

3  Tablespoons  parsley 

Saute  the  rice  in  butter  in  heavy  frying  pan 
2-3  minutes,  stirring  often.   Stir  in  onions, 
juice,  bouillon.   Cover  tightly.   Bake  at 
350°  for  30  minutes.   Stir,  cover  and  bake 
30  minutes  longer.   Serves  6.

Spinach 

1  teaspoon  minced  onion 

2  bags  fresh  spinach,  washed  and 

coarsely  chopped 
3/4  cup  hot  water 
2  Tablespoons  thick  cream 
2  Tablespoons  butter 
Pinch  nutmeg 

Cook  spinach  and  onion  in  hot  water.   Cook 
5 ' minutes .   Remove  spinach.   Reduce  liquid 
to  1  tablespoon.   Add  cream,  butter  and

Summer  Squash,  Baked 

8  small  squash 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

1  cup  sour  cream 

h    teaspoon  allspice 

1  can  chopped  pimiento  with  juice 

h    cup  grated  Swiss  cheese 

h    cup  dry  sherry 

Salt  and  pepper 

Scrub  the  squash,  and  steam  for  20  minutes, 
or  until  barely  tender.   Cut  in  half  and 
arrange  side  by  side  in  well  buttered  baking 
dish.   While  squash  is  cooking,  prepare 
sauce.   Melt  butter,  blend  in  sour  cream, 
allspice,  pimiento,  cheese,  sherry,  salt 
and  pepper.   Stir  till  smooth.   Pour  over 
the  squash.   Bake  15  minutes  at  350°.   Serve 
immediately.   Serves  8.

Chicken.  Salad  in  Cranberry  Ring 


1%  cups  sliced  fresh  peaches 
3  cups  cooked  chicken,  cubed 
1  cup  celery,  diced 

cup  mayonnaise 

Tablespoons  salad  oil 

Tablespoon  vinegar 

teaspoon  salt 

cup  coarsely  broken  pecans,  toasted 

cup  orange  juice 

cup  water 

3-oz  .  packages  lemon  gelatin 

teaspoon  salt 

cup  orange  juice 

can  whole  cramberry  sauce  (1  lb.) 


Heat  1  cup  orange  juice  and  water  to  boiling. 
Add  gelatin  and  salt.  Stir  till  dissolved. 
Stir  in  second  cup  of  orange  juice.  Chill  till 
partially  set.  Stir  in  cranberry  sauce.  Pour 
into  6^  cup  mold.  Chill  6  to  8  hours.  Unmold 
on  plate.  Set  aside  a  few  peach  slices  for 
garnish.  In  large  bowl,  combine  remaining 
peach  slices,  chicken  and  celery.  In  small 
bowl  combine  mayonnaise,  salad  oil,  vinegar 
and  salt.  Pour  dressing  over  chicken  mixture. 
Toss  lightly.  Chill.  Just  before  serving" 
stir  in  pecans.  Toss  again.  Serve  in  cran- 
berry ring.  Garnish  with  reserved  peach  slices 
Serves  8-10. 


Pep  up  chicken-celery  salad  with  capers  and 
use  some  of  the  juice  from  the  bottle  or  add 
extra  vinegar  to  the  mayonnaise.

Summer  Salmon  Mousse 

2  1-lb.  cans  red  salmon 

2  envelopes  gelatin 

^  cup  cold  water 

lh    cups  fish  juice  +  water 

2  bouillon  cubes 

1  teaspoon  salt 
h    cup  vinegar 

h    cup  lemon  juice 

2  Tablespoons  sugar 

2  teaspoons  grated  onion 

2  teaspoons  prepared  horseradish 

1  1/3  cups  mayonnaise 

1  cup  chopped  ripe  olives 

Drain  and  flake  salmon.  Soften  gelatin  in 
cold  water.  Add  the  water  to  the  juice  to 
make  1%.    cups,  heat  with  bouillon  cubes  to 
boiling.  Add  gelatin  and  stir  until  dis- 
solved. Add  salt,  vinegar,  lemon,  sugar, 
onion,  horseradish.  Cool  until  gelatin 
thickens  slightly.  Blend  in  mayonnaise, 
olives  and  salmon.  Turn  into  6-cup  mold 
and  chill  till  firm.  Unmold  and  garnish 
with  sliced  cucumbers  and  tomato  wedges. 
Serve  with  avocado  cream.  Serves  10-12. 

Avocado  Cream 

h    avocado,  sieved 
h    cup  sour  cream

wheat  in  a  strainer  until  it  is  very  dry.

wheat  and  stir  until  thoroughly  mixed.

Tomato-Dill  Aspic  with  Artichoke  Hearts 

3  envelopes  gelatin 

%  cup  tomato  juice 

5  cups  +  2  teaspoons  tomato 

1/3  cup  lemon  juice 

1  Tablespoon  grated  onion 

1  clove  garlic,  crushed 

2  teaspoons  dried  dill 
2  teaspoons  salt 

1  teaspoon  basil 

1  teaspoon  oregano 

1  bay  leaf,  crushed 

1  19-oz.  can  artichoke  hearts 

Soften  gelatin  in  \    cup  tomato  juice. 
Heat  the  rest  of  the  tomato  juice,  lemon 
juice,  onion,  garlic,  dill,  salt,  basil, 
oregano  and  bay  leaf.   Simmer  together 
for  10  minutes.   Remove  from  heat  and 
strain  through  cheese  cloth.   Add  softened 
gelatin  and  stir  till  dissolved.   Cool. 
Drain  artichoke  hearts  and  slice  in  half. 
In  bottom  of  a  two-quart  mold,  arrange 
design  of  artichoke  hearts.   To  seal  in 
the  design,  carefully  add  enough  of  the 
tomato  mixture  to  measure  about  VT  deep 
in  the  bottom  of  the  mold  and  chill  until 
gelatin  is  thickened  but  not  firm.   Add 
remaining  artichoke  hearts  and  tomato  juice 
mixture  and  chill  until  firm.   Unmold  and 
garnish  with  crisp  greens  and  serve  with 
caviar  mayonnaise.   Serves  10-12.

Caviar  Mayonnaise 

1  cup  mayonnaise 
1  cup  sour  cream 

1  Tablespoon  lemon  juice 

2  teaspoons  prepared  mustard 

1  oz .  jar  black  caviar 

Mix  well  together  the  mayonnaise,  sour 
cream,  lemon  juice  and  mustard.  Fold  in 
the  caviar.  Makes  about  1  3/4  cups.  Serve 
with  Tomato-Dill  Aspic. 

Tomato-Shrimp  Aspic 

2  envelopes  gelatin 
^  cup  tomato  juice 
3h    cups  tomato  juice 

h    clove  garlic,  peeled 

1  bay  leaf 

Dash  of  Worcestershire 

2  Tablespoons  grated  onion 
3/4  cup  chopped  celery 

h    cup  olives,  drained  and  chopped 
2  cups  cooked  shrimp 

Soften  gelatin  in  the  %    cup  tomato  juice. 
Heat  the  rest  of  the  tomato  juice  with  the 
garlic,  bay  leaf,  and  Worcestershire  just 
to  the  boiling  point.  Remove  garlic  and 
bay  leaf  and  stir  in  the  softened  gelatin 
and  stir  till  dissolved.  Cool  slightly  and 
add  the  onion,  celery,  olives  and  shrimp. 
Pour  into  a  greased  mold  to  set.  Serves  6. 

Carolyn  Bates

Herb  Casserole  Bread 

%  cup  milk 

2  Tablespoons  sugar 

1  teaspoon  salt 

1  Tablespoon  butter 

2  Tablespoons  finely  chopped  oniftn 
1  teaspoon  leaf  oregano,  crumbled 
H    teaspoon  leaf  marjoram,  crumbled 
h    cup  warm  water 

1  package  dry  yeast 

1  egg 

2  or  more  cups  sifted  flour 

Combine  milk,  sugar,  salt,  butter,  onion, 
oregano,  marjoram  in  saucepan.   Heat  till 
bubbles  appear  and  shortening  is  melted. 
Cool  to  lukewarm.   Measure  warm  water  into 
medium  size  mixing  bowl;  sprinkle  in  yeast 
Stir  to  dissolve.   Add  lukewarm  milk  mix- 
ture.  Stir  in  egg.   Add  1  cup  flour  or 
enough  to  make  a  thick  batter.   Beat 
vigorously  until  mixture  is  well  blended. 
Stir  in  eough  flour  to  make  a  stiff  batter 
Beat  until  well  blended.   Cover;  let  rise 
in  warm  place  about  50  or  60  minutes  until 
doubled  in  bulk.   Stir  batter  down.   Turn 
into  well  greased  lh    quart  casserole.   Let 
rise  30  minutes.   Bake  at  350°  for  45  to 
50  minutes  or  until  well  browned.   Remove 
from  oven;  allow  to  cool  in  casserole  for 

3  minutes.   Remove  from  casserole;  cool 
thoroughly  on  wire  rack. 

Carol  Rice

Jiffy  Orange  Nut  Bread 

2  cups  sifted  flour 

1  teaspoon  baking  powder 

1  teaspoon  soda 

1  teaspoon  salt 

2  Tablespoons  butter 
^  cup  boiling  water 
1/3  cup  orange  juice 

1  cup  sugar 

2  teaspoons  vanilla 

1  slightly  beaten  egg 

%  cup  coarsely  chopped  nuts 

Walnut  halves 

Mix  the  dry  ingredients.  Melt  the  butter 
in  the  boiling  water  in  medium  size  bowl. 
Blend  the  orange  juice,  sugar,  vanilla  and 
egg.  Sift  dry  ingredients  over  orange  mix- 
ture, add  nuts.  Stir  just  until  the  flour 
is  dampened.  Pour  into  loaf  pan,  decorate 
with  walnut  halves.  Bake  one  hour  at  350°. 

Christina  Ewen

Rolls 

1  package  dry  yeast 

1  heaping  teaspoon  salt 

3  Tablespoons  sugar 

1  egg 

1  stick  butter 

1  cup  milk 

1  cup  water 

Flour,  at  least  4  cups 

Put  1  tablespoon  sugar  into  1  cup  warm 
water  and  dissolve  yeast  in  this.   Add 
salt,  2  tablespoons  sugar  and  butter  to 
milk  and  heat  to  boiling.   Cool.   Beat 
egg.   Combine  egg,  yeast  and  milk  mix- 
ture and  beat  in  4  cups  of  flour.   Add 
more  flour  as  needed.   When  too  stiff 
to  beat  with  a  spoon,  turn  out  on  floured 
board  and  work  flour  into  mixture  until  a 
firm  dough  but  not  too  stiff.   Let  rise 
in  a  warm  place  until  double,  about  2 
hours.   Make  into  pocketbook  rolls  by 
hand.   Let  rise  until  double,  about  2 
hours.   Bake  in  400°  oven  for  about  10 
minutes  depending  on  how  brown  you  wish 
them.   When  reheating  set  oven. at  350°. 
They  freeze  well.   Also  keep  well  in 
plastic  bags  in  the  refrigerator. 

Elizabeth  Carr 
Cheese  Rolls 

Heat  oven  to  350.  Remove  crusts  from  thin 
slices  of  fresh  bread.  Spread  with  softened 
butter  and  sprinkle  with  grated  cheese.  Roll 
up,  fasten  with  toothpicks  and  toast  in  oven 
until  lightly  browned.

h    lb.  butter  (no  substitute) 

h    cup  sugar 

2^  cups  sifted  flour

about  h"    thick.  Prick  with  fork  as  for  a  pie 
shell.  Bake  45  minutes  at  275°,  turning  pan 
every  15  minutes.  Cut  while  hot  but  leave  in 
pan  until  cold.

2H    cups  boiling  water 

2  Tablespoons  melted  fat 

lh    Tablespoons  salt 

2  eggs 

\\    cups  buttermilk 

1  teaspoon  soda 

Stir  corn  meal  gradually  into  boiling  water. 
Let  stand  till  cool.   Separate  the  eggs, 
beat  yolks  and  stir  into  corn  meal  with  the 
fat,  salt  and  milk  in  which  the  soda  has 
been  dissolved.   Add  the  egg  whites,  beaten 
stiff.   Pour  into  greased  baking  dish.   Bake 
in  425°  oven  for  40  minutes.

Angel  Pie 

4  eggs,  separated 

\    teaspoon  cream  of  tartar 

1  cup  sugar 
\    cup  sugar 

3  Tablespoons  lemon  juice 

2  teaspoons  grated  lemon  peel 
Jg  teaspoon  vanilla 

1  cup  whipping  cream 

Beat  egg  whites  until  frothy.  Add  cream  of 
tartar  and  beat  until  stiff.  Slowly  add  1 
cup  sugar,  beating  until  glossy.  Spread  in 
well  greased  deep  pie  pan.  Bake  at  275°  for 
nearly  2  hours.  Cool.  Beat  egg  yolks,  slowly 
beating  in  \    cup  sugar,  lemon  juice  and  peel 
Cook  in  top  of  double  boiler  until  thick. 
Cool.  Add  vanilla  to  cream  and  whip  until 
stiff.  Put  together  in  layers;  meringue, 
half  the  cream,  custard,  remaining  cream. 
Refrigerate  for  24  hours. 

Helen  Masur

2  cups  sugar 

4  lemons 

1  can  No.  2  apricots 
1  Tablespoon  gelatine 

Dissolve  gelatine  in  2  Tablespoons  cold  water

Juice  of  1  lemon

Chocolate  Marshmallow

1^  cups  milk 

4  Tablespoons  cocoa 

^  teaspoon  salt 

2  Tablespoons  rum 

20  oz .  whipping  cream 

2  teaspoons  vanilla 

In  the  top  of  a  double  boiler  cook  the 
marshmallows,  milk,  cocoa  and  salt  until 
the  marshmallows  dissolve.  Cool  and  add

mixture  slowly.  Continue  beating  till 
well  mixed.  Pour  into  individual  serving

chill  till  ready  to  serve.  Serves  6.

Creme  Bruise 

2  cups  sweet  cream 

8  Tablespoons  brown  or  maple  sugar 

4  egg  yolks  beaten  till  frothy 

Scald  in  double  boiler  2  cups  cream  and  2 
Tablespoons  of  the  sugar.   Combine  %  cup  of 
this  heated  cream  with  egg  yolks.   Return 
this  mixture  to  double  boiler  and  cook  till 
it  thickens  slightly  and  mixture  coats  the 
spoon.   Pour  into  custard  cups,  cool  in  re- 
frigerator until  set.   When  set,  sprinkle 
top  with  brown  or  maple  sugar,  about  V 
thick.   Place  under  broiler  until  sugar 
caramelizes.   Do  not  scorch.   Cool  again 
and  refrigerate. 

Kathy  Barnes 

Creme  renversee 

4  eggs 

1/3  cup  sugar 

2  cups  warm  milk 

2  teaspoons  vanilla  or  1  almond,  1  vanilla 

10  lumps  or  %  cup  sugar 

2  Tablespoons  water 

Beat  eggs  with  sugar,  add  milk  and  flavoring. 
Do  not  beat  hard.   Place  sugar  lumps  or  %  cup 
sugar'  and  2  Tablespoons  water  in  the  mold  in 
which  you  will  make  the  custard.   Heat  till 
golden  brown,  watching  constantly.   Remove 
from  stove  and  turn  the  mold  so  the  caramel 
coats  the  inside  well.   Pour  egg  mixture  into 
mold  and  bake  at  350°  (with  the  mold  resting 
in  a  pan  of  hot  water)  40  minutes  or  longer. 
It  is  done  when  a  knife  inserted  in  it  comes 
out  clear. 

Denise  Limouze

2/3  cup  sugar 
3/4  cup  sweet  sherry 
h    teaspoon  salt 

Mix  egg  yolks  and  sugar  in  top  of  a  lh    quart 
double  boiler.   Set  over  simmering  water  and 
beat  with  rotary  beater  till  fluffy.   Add 
sherry  gradually  and  continue  beating  till 
mixture  resembles  whipped  cream.   Cool  and

2)  garnish  with  cherries. 
Serves  6 .

Lemon  Chiffon  Pie 

1  envelope  gelatine 

1  cup  sugar 

1/8  teaspoon  salt 

4  eggs,  separated 
^  cup  lemon  juice 
h    cup  water 

2  teaspoons  lemon  peel 
9"  baked  pie  shell 

Mix  gelatine,  h    cup  sugar  and  salt  in  the  top 
of  a  double  boiler.   Beat  egg  yolks,  lemon 
juice  and  water  together  and  add  to  gelatine. 
Cook  over  boiling  water  till  gelatine  is  dis- 
solved.  Remove  from  heat  and  add  lemon  peel. 
Chill,  stirring  occasionally  till  mixture 
mounds  slightly  when  dropped  from  a  spoon. 
Beat  egg  whites  till  stiff  and  beat  in  remain- 
ing sugar.   Fold  egg  whites  into  gelatine  mix- 
ture.  Turn  into  baked  pie  shell  and  chill  till 
firm.   Serves  6 . 

Marie  Th^rese  Sommerville

Lime  Sherbet 

1  package  lime  gelatine 
1  cup  boiling  water 

1  cup  sugar 

2  lemons,  juice  and  grated  rind 
1  quart  of  milk 

Dissolve  the  gelatine  in  the  boiling  water. 
Add  sugar  and  stir  until  dissolved.   Add  the 
juice  and  grated  rind  of  the  lemons.   When 
cool,  add  milk  slowly  and  pour  into  freezing 
tray  of  refrigerator.   As  it  freezes,  stir 
with  a  fork.

3/4  cup  cold  water 
2/3  cup  sugar 

h    teaspoon  salt 

3/4  cup  boiling  water 

2/3  cup  lemon  juice 

1  cup  orange  juice 

Bananas 

Sprinkle  the  gelatin  over  the  3/4  cup  cold 
water.  Add  the  sugar,  salt  and  boiling 
water.  Stir  until  the  gelatin  is  dissolved. 
Add  lemon  juice  and  orange  juice.  Cool. 
Pour  half  of  the  gelatin  mixture  over  sliced

gelatin  on  top.  Serve  with  whipped  cream.

Poached  Pears  with  creme  anglaise 

6  Anjou  or  Bosc  pears,  slightly  under  ripe 
4  cups  water 

2  cups  sugar 

1  Tablespoon  lemon  juice 
1  teaspoon  lemon  rind 
1  stick  cinnamon 

3  whole  cloves 

Bring  to  a  boil  sugar,  water,  lemon  juice 
and  rind.  Add  pears  and  spices.  Cover  and 
keep  at  rolling  boil  until  pears  are  ten- 
der -  about  30  minutes.  Stand  pears  up  in 
shallow  dish  in  a  little  syrup.  Cover  and 
chill.  Cover  x^ith  creme  anglaise  at  the 
last  minute  before  serving. 

Ellen  Bates 

Creme  anglaise 

1  cup  milk 

^  cup  heavy  cream 

1  vanilla  bean  or  1  teaspoon  vanilla  extract 
6  Tablespoons  sugar 

4  large  egg  yolks 

2  teaspoons  cornstarch 

Combine  milk,  cream  and  vanilla,  bring  just 
to  a  boil  and  let  stand  10  minutes.  Gradually 
beat  sugar  into  yolks  and  continue  beating 
for  3  minutes  until  pale  yellow  and  creamy. 
Beat  in  cornstarch.  Stir  milk  and  cream  into 
yolks  and  beat  with  a  whisk.  Return  to  sauce- 
pan and  cook  over  low  heat,  stirring  with  a 
wooden  spoon  until  quite  thick  (about  15 
minutes).  Do  not  let  it  boil.  Cool,  stir- 
ring frequently,  cover  and  chill.  Pour  over 
pears  just  before  serving. 

Ellen  Bates

4  eggs 

1  cup  milk 

3/4  cup  sugar

Pineapple  Tarts  Alaskan 

h    cup  sugar 

1  Tablespoon  cornstarch 

h    teaspoon  salt 

#2  can  crushed  pineapple 

1  pint  vanilla  ice  cream 
3  egg  whites 

6  Tablespoons  sugar  for  meringue 
12  tart  shells  made  on  the  back  of  large 
muffin  tins 

Mix  the  sugar,  cornstarch  and  salt  in  a 
saucepan.   Add  the  pineapple,  stirring  con- 
stantly.  Cook  until  clear  and  slightly 
thick  (about  5  minutes).   Cool  and  chill. 
Make  meringue  by  beating  the  egg  whites  until 
stiff  and  adding  the  sugar  gradually;  beat 
until  meringue  stands  in  peaks.   When  ready 
to  serve  the  tarts  pre-heat  oven  to  500°. 
Place  tart  shells  on  cookie  sheet;  fill  with 
pineapple  mixture,  place  ice  cream  in  each, 
spread  meringue  on  each  so  that  it  sticks 
to  the  crust  all  the  way  around  and  bake 

2  or  3  minutes  or  until  brown.   Serve  at 
once .

ture will  not  freeze  solid.

Strawberry  Cheesecake  Surprise

2  Tablespoons  sugar 

1  cup  boiling  water 
h    cup  cold  water 

2  cups  strawberries,  sliced 

1  package  jello  cheesecake  mix 

Dissolve  jello  and  sugar  in  boiling  water. 
Add  cold  water  and  strawberries.  Chill  till 
thickened.  Pour  into  a  lightly  oiled  1^ 
quart  mold.  Chill  till  set.  Prepare  cheese- 
cake filling  as  directed  on  the  package. 
Spread  evenly  over  the  jello.  Chill.

filling.  Chill  three  hours  or  more.  Unmold. 
Serves  8-10.

Woodford  Pudding 

3  eggs 

1  cup  sugar 

h    cup  butter  (1  stick) 

1  cup  strawberry  or  apricot  preserves 

1  teaspoon  soda 

3  Tablespoons  sour  milk 

H    teaspoon  nutmeg 

^  teaspoon  cinnamon 

1  cup  flour 

Beat  eggs  slightly.  Add  sugar,  butter  (rubbed 
to  a  cream)  ,  preserves  ,  soda  dissolved  in  the 
sour  milk,  spices  and  flour.  Mix  well.  Bake 
in  buttered  pudding  dish  at  325°  for  an  hour 
or  until  firm.  Serve  with  cream,  sweetened 
and  flavored  with  sherry.

Zabaglione 

4  egg  yolks 

2  Tablespoons  powdered  sugar 

2  Tablespoons  Marsala  wine 

Beat  egg  yolks  with  sugar  until  thick  and 
lemon-colored.  Put  in  double  boiler  over 
hot,  not  boiling  water.  Beat  constantly, 
adding  wine  little  by  little,  until  mix- 
ture is  beginning  to  hold  its  shape  but 
is  still  smooth.  Remove  from  heat  and  pile 
immediately  into  dessert  glasses.  Serve 
warm  or  very  cold  with  simple  wafer.  Serves 
2  or  3. 

Gertrude  Marchetti 

Sherry  Chocolate  Pudding 

1  package  chocolate  pudding  mix 
1  1/3  cups  rich  milk 
%  cup  sherry 

Combine  mix  and  milk  and  cook  according  to 
package  directions.  Remove  from  heat,  stir 
in  sherry  and  pour  into  sherbet  glasses. 
Serve  with  whipped  cream  or  topping  and 
sprinkle  with  cinnamon.  Serves  4.

Lemon  Sauce 

2  whole  lemons 
\    cup  sugar 
%  cup  water 
6  whole  eggs 
%  cup  sugar 

Into  a  large  pan,  grate  the  whole  lemons. 
Remove  the  seeds  after  grating.  Add  the 
sugar  and  water.  Cook  3  minutes  or  until 
boiling.  Beat  the  eggs  until  light  and 
fluffy.  Add  the  other  ^  cup  sugar  to  the 
eggs.  Slowly  add  the  egg  mixture  to  the 
lemon  mixture,  stirring  constantly.  Cook 
until  it  thickens.  Remove  from  fire  and 
cool.  When  cool,  pour  into  container  and 
refrigerate.  This  sauce  is  good  on  sponge 
cake,  gingerbread,  etc. 

Phyllis  Cohn 


Strawberry  Sauce 

2  cups  strawberries 
%.    cup  powdered  sugar 
1  teaspoon  lemon  juice 
1  egg  white 
1/8  teaspoon  salt 

Hull  the  strawberries,  then  mash  with  a 
silver  fork.  Add  sugar  and  lemon  juice. 
Whip  the  egg  white  and  salt  together  un- 
til stiff.  Add  to  the  strawberry  mixture 
Whip  sauce  until  it  is  light  and  fluffy. 
Good  served  over  angel  food  cake. 

Elizabeth  Carr

Apple  Cake 

\    cup  shortening 
1  cup  sugar 

1  egg ,  beaten 

2  cups  chopped  apples 
^  teaspoon  salt 

1  cup  flour,  sifted 

1  teaspoon  soda 

3/4  teaspoon  cinnamon 

1  cup  chopped  nuts  or  raisins  (Optional) 

Sour  Cream 

Cream  sugar  and  shortening  together.   Add 
egg.   Beat  well.   Stir  in  chopped  apples. 
Sift  dry  ingredients  together,  add  to  mix- 
ture in  thirds.   Beat  until  blended.   Do 
not  overheat.   Stir  in  nuts  and/or  raisins 
Turn  into  a  greased  and  floured  8"x8"x2" 
cake  pan.   Bake  at  350°  for  45  minutes. 
Cut  in  squares  and  serve  warm  or  cold  with 
a  dollop  of  sour  cream  on  top. 

Helen  Garland 


To  avoid  smearing  the  plate  when  frosting 
a  cake,  place  a  circular  piece  of  waxed 
paper  around  the  edge.   When  cake  is  frosted, 
pull  out  the  paper. 


Brown  sugar  will  not  become  lumpy  if  a 
piece  of  blotting  paper  is  fitted  to  the 
inside  of  the  lid.

h    cup  butter  ! 

3/4  cup  sugar 

1  large  egg,  beaten 

2  cups  unsifted  flour 

2  teaspoons  baking  powder 

^  cup  milk 

2  cups  blueberries 

Topping: 

^  cup  sugar 

2  teaspoons  cinnamon 

%    cup  nuts 

2  Tablespoons  flour 

3  Tablespoons  butter 

Cream  the  butter  and  sugar.  Add  the  beaten 
egg.  Add  the  dry  ingredients  alternately 
with  the  milk.  Blend.  Fold  in  the  blueberries. 
Pour  into  a  square  cake  pan.  Top  with  mix 
made  from  other  ingredients  ,  mixed  till 
crumbly.  Bake  at  375°  for  45  to  50  minutes. 
Serve  warm.

Chocolate  Pound  Cake 


3  cups  sugar 

\    lb .  but  t er 

^  cup  vegetable  shortening 

6  eggs 

3  cups  flour 

\    teaspoon  baking  powder 

4  Tablespoons  cocoa 
1  cup  milk 

1  Tablespoon  vanilla 

Cream  butter,  sugar  and  vegetable  shorten 
ing.  A*dd  eggs  and  beat.  Add  sifted  dry  in 
gredients  alternately  with  milk.  Add 
vanilla.  Pour  in  greased  and  floured  tube 
pan.  Bake  in  preheated  oven  at  350°  for

Chocolate  Cake 

1  cup  Hellman's  mayonnaise 

1  cup  sugar 

2  cups  flour 

lh    teaspoons  soda 

lh    teaspoons  baking  powder 

4  Tablespoons  cocoa 

1  cup  water 

2  teaspoons  vanilla 

Blend  together  the  mayonnaise  and  sugar.  Add 
alternately  the  wet  and  dry  ingredients.  Mix 
until  smooth.  Pour  into  a  9"x9"  pan  which 
has  been  lightly  greased.  Bake  at  350°  for 
35  to  40  minutes  or  until  inserted  straw 
comes  out  clean.  Frost,  with  Frosting  for 
Chocolate  Cake. 

Sarah  Watson 

Frosting  for  Chocolate  Cake 

h    cup  butter 

2  cups  sugar 

%    cup  milk 

h    cup  cocoa 

2  teaspoons  vanilla 

Put  all  the  ingredients,  except  the  vanilla, 
into  a  saucepan.  Bring  to  a  boil  and  boil  2 
minutes.  Stir  until  partly  cool.  Add  the 
vanilla.  Pour  over  the  cake  while  the  cake 
is  still  a  bit  warm.  (It  may  take  a  while 
for  the  cake  to  absorb  the  full  amount  of 
frosting . ) 

Sarah  Watson

Chocolate  Almond  Cake 

9  eggs ,  separated 
6  squares  semi-sweet  chocolate 
6  oz.  grated  almonds,  unblanched 
6  oz.  XXXX  sugar 

6  whole  eggs 

7  oz.  XXXX  sugar 

7  oz.  semi-sweet  chocolate 
7  oz.  unsalted  butter 

Cream  9  egg  yolks  and  sugar  until  thick  and 
light  in  color.   Melt  chocolate.   Beat  9  egg 
whites  till  stiff.   Butter  10"  pan  and  dust 
with  flour.   Mix  egg  yolks,  sugar  with 
chocolate,  almonds  and  sugar  till  smooth. 
Fold  in  egg  whites.   Bake  in  preheated  350° 
oven  for  50-55  minutes.   Cool  and  refrigerate 
overnight.   To  make  filling:   Cream  6  eggs 
with  sugar  in  a  double  boiler  above  steam 
until  thick.   Remove  and  mix  in  the  7  oz . 
melted  chocolate.   Cool  overnight.   Next 
day:   Cream  unsalted  butter.   When  fluffy, 
mix  in  the  creamed  chocolate,  sugar  and 
eggs.   Take  cake  from  the  refrigerator. 
Slice  with  thin  bread  knife  into  4  layers. 
Fill  with  chocolate  cream  and  cover  top  and 
sides.   Refrigerate  but  do  not  freeze. 

Iren  Marik

Chocolate  Toffee  Angel  Food  Cake 

1  pint  whipping  cream 

5h    oz.  can  Hersheys  chocolate  syrup 

1  Angel  food  cake 

%    lb.  English  toffee,  .crushed 

h    teaspoon  vanilla 

Whip  the  cream  until  it  starts  to  thicken. 
Gradually  pour  in  the  chocolate  syrup  and 
vanilla  and  continue  beating  until  cream  is 
thick.   Cut  cake  into  4  layers.   Spread 
each  layer  with  the  chocolate  cream, 
sprinkle  toffee  over  the  cream  on  each 
layer.   Frost  the  top  and  sides  of  cake 
with  remaining  cream.   Sprinkle  top  with 
candy.   Refrigerate  at  least  2  hours  be- 
fore serving. 

Lucy  Lombardi 

Grandmother  Smith's  Cake 

1  box  powdered  sugar 

3  sticks  butter 

6  eggs 

3  cups  sifted  cake  flour 

Cream  sugar  and  butter.   Beat  the  eggs  in, 
one  at  a  time.   Beat  well  after  each  addition 
Add  the  sifted  flour  slowly,  mixing  until 
thoroughly  blended.   Pour  the  batter  into 
a  greased  tube  pan  and  bake  at  350°  for 
approximately  1  hour. 

Jan    Sheets

1  stick  butter 

4  Tablespoons  cocoa 

1  cup  water 

2  cups  granulated  sugar 
2  cups  flour 

2  eggs 

H    cup  buttermilk 

1  teaspoon  soda 

%  teaspoon  salt 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

1  teaspoon  cinnamon 


1  stick  butter 
4  Tablespoons  cocoa 
6  Tablespoons  milk 
1  lb.  XXXX  sugar 
1  teaspoon  vanilla 
1  cup  chopped  pecans 

Bring  to  a  boil  the  butter,  cocoa,  water, 
stirring  occasionally.   Sift  together  in 
mixer  bowl,  sugar  and  flour.   Add  cocoa 
mixture  and  beat,  adding  eggs,  buttermilk, 
soda,  salt,  vanilla  and  cinnamon.   Pour 
into  oiled  and  floured  jelly  roll  pan 
(lSVxIOV'xl")  and  bake  for  20  minutes  at 
400°.   While  cake  is  baking  make  icing. 
...  Bring  to  a  boil  the  butter,  cocoa,  milk, 
stirring  constantly.   Pour  this  over  powdered 
sugar.   Add  vanilla  and  pecans.   Stir  until 
blended.   Remove  cake  from  oven  and  spread 
icing  over  hot  cake  while  it  is  still  in 
pan.   Cool  and  cut  in  squares.

Glazed  Pineapple  Carrot  Cake

lh    cups  sugar

2  teaspoons  cinnamon 
h    teaspoon  salt 

3  eggs 

h    cup  salad  oil 
3/4  cup  buttermilk 
2  teaspoons  vanilla 

1  can  (8%  oz.)  crushed  pineapple,  well  drained 

2  cups  finely  shredded  carrots 
1  cup  coarsely  chopped  nuts 

1  cup  flaked  cocoanut

together.  Beat  eggs  and  oil  together  with 
the  buttermilk  and  vanilla.  Add  to  the  dry 
ingredients  and  beat  till  smooth.  Mix  in 
pineapple,  carrots,  nuts  and  cocoanut.  Bake 
in  lightly  greased  and  floured  pan  9nxl3"  at 
350°  for  45  minutes.  Remove  and  lightly  prick 
with  fork.

Strawberry  Cake

1  package  wild  strawberry  jello 

1  package  frozen  strawberries 
3/4  cup  salad  oil 

4  eggs 

2  teaspoons  lemon  juice 
1  cup  XXXX  sugar 

Mix  jello  with  cake  mix. Add  thawed  strawberries 
except  for  2  Tablespoons.   Add  oil  and  beat  in 
eggs,  one  at  a  time.   Bake  in  tube  pan  at  350° 
for  about  one  hour.   Remove  from  oven  and  let 
rest  for  15  minutes.   Remove  from  pan  and  glaze 
with  a  glaze  made  from  XXXX  sugar  and  lemon 
juice  and  reserved  strawberries.

Italian  Cream  Cake 

h  lb.  butter 

%  cup  shortening 

2  cups  sugar 

5  egg  yolks 

1  cup  buttermilk 

2  cups  flour 

1  teaspoon  soda 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

1  cup  nuts 

5  egg  whites,  stiffly  beaten

to  chill  bowl  and  beaters  in  refrigerator 
for  10  minutes  before  using  them.

and  put  in  dollops  on  a  piece  of  waxed  paper. 
The  dollops  can  then  be  frozen  and  when  stiff, 
put  into  proper  containers.

Stuffed  Angel  Food  Cake 

1  large  angel  food  cake 
5g  cup  sugar 

1/3  cup  flour 
^  teaspoon  salt 

2  cups  milk,  scalded 

2  eggs,  lightly  beaten 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

1  cup  blanched,  chopped  almonds 

1  Tablespoon  rum 

Whipped  cream 

Combine  sugar,  flour,  salt  in  small  bowl. 
Add  milk  and  stir  till  smooth  and  thick. 
Pour  these  ingredients  over  eggs.  Stir  and 
cook  the  custard  in  a  double  boiler  over 
hot,  not  boiling  water,  till  the  eggs  thicken 
Cool  mixture  and  add  vanilla,  almonds  and  rum 
Prepare  cake  by  cutting  in  two  layers,  1/3 
way  down  from  the  top.  Dig  a  1"  trench  in  the 
bottom  layer.  Fill  trench  with  the  cooled  cus 
tard.  Replace  top  layer  of  cake.  Ice  cake 
with  whipped  cream.  Sprinkle  with  nuts  and 
chill  thoroughly  before  serving. 


Lucy  Lombardi 


A  quick,  easy  and  delicious  frosting  for 
angel  food  cake  may  be  made  by  adding  an 
envelope  of  instant  hot  cocoa  mix  to  a  10 
ounce  carton  of  non-dairy  whipped  topping. 


225 


Yule  Cake 

1^  cups  shelled  Brazil  nuts 

1^  cups  shelled  walnut  halves 

1  cup  pitted  dates 

1  cup  chopped  candied  orange  peel 

H    cup  red  maraschino  cherries 

H    cup  green  maraschino  cherries 

%  cup  seedless  raisins 

3/4  cups  sifted  flour 

3/4  cup  sugar 

h    teaspoon  salt 

H    teaspoon  baking  powder 

3  eggs 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

Grease  a  loaf  pan,  9"x5"x3M,  line  bottom 
and  ends  with  wax  paper.   Grease  paper. 
Combine  nuts  and  fruit  in  large  bowl.   Mix 
flour,  sugar,  baking  powder,  and  salt  and 
sift  over  fruit  mix.   Mix  well.   Beat  eggs 
till  fluffy,  stir  in  vanilla.   Pour  over 
fruit  mixture.   Fold  in  thoroughly.   Spoon 
into  pan,  pressing  down  firmly  with  a  spoon 
to  make  top  even.   Bake  in  a  slow  oven,  300 
for  about  1-3/4  hours,  or  until  a  long  thin 
skewer  inserted  in  center  comes  out  clean. 
Cool  cake  in  pan  on  wire  rack  10  minutes  . 
Loosen  around  edges  with  a  knife,  turn  out 
onto  rack.   Peel  off  paper.   Cool  completely. 
To  store,  slide  cake  into  a  plastic  bag  and 
seal.   It  will  keep  fresh  and  moist  in  the 
refrigerator  for  about  8  weeks,  or  in  the 
freezer,  for  three  months. 

Phyllis  Cohn

^  teaspoon  baking  powder

Butter  Cookies 

h    cup  butter 

H    cup  sugar 

1  egg  yolk 

h    teaspoon  vanilla 

lh    cups  flour 

5g  teaspoon  baking  powder 

1/8  teaspoon  salt 

3  teaspoons  milk  or  cream 

Cream  shortening,  add  sugar  and  mix  thor- 
oughly. Add  unbeaten  egg  yolk  and  vanilla 
Stir  together  thoroughly.  Sift  baking  pow

cream  mixture  alternately  with  the  milk.

Congo  Bars 

2  3/4  cups  flour 

2\    teaspoons  baking  powder 

%  teaspoon  salt 

2/3  cup  shortening 

1  package  dark  brown  sugar 

3  eggs 

1  large  package  chocolate  bits  (12  oz.) 
1  teaspoon  vanilla 

Sift  together  the  flour,  baking  powder  and 
salt.  Cream  the  shortening  with  the  sugar. 
Add  the  eggs,  one  at  a  time,  beating  well 
after  each  addition.  Add  the  dry  ingredients 
and  blend  well.  Fold  in  the  chocolate  bits 
and  vanilla.  Spread  on  a  well  greased  cookie 
sheet,  10V'xl5^"x  3/4".  Bake  at  350°  for  35 
minutes.  Cool  and  slice  in  bars.

Cream  Cheese  Cookies 

^  lb .  butter 

8  oz.  package  cream  cheese 

2  cups  sifted  flour 

Cinnamon 

Sugar 

Chopped  walnuts 

Rais  ins 

Combine  butter  and  cheese  with  the  flour  to 
make  a  dough.   Place  in  refrigerator  to 
chill.   Divide  dough  into  4  or  5  pieces. 
Roll  each  piece  as  thin  as  desired.   Sprinkle 
with  cinnamon  and  sugar  and  chopped  walnuts 
and  raisins.   Roll  as  you  would  a  jelly  roll. 
Dip  silver  knife  in  water  and  cut  the  roll 
into  cookies.   Place  on  the  cookie  sheet, 
standing  up.   Sprinkle  tops  with  cinnamon 
and  sugar.   Bake  12  to  15  minutes,  until 
golden  brown,  at  350°.

Lemon  Squares 

2  cups  flour 
%  cup  sugar 

1  cup  butter 

2  cups  sugar 

1  teaspoon  baking  powder 
4  Tablespoons  flour 

3  eggs,  beaten 

Juice  and  grated  rind  of  2  lemons 
Powdered  sugar  (optional) 

Mix  the  flour,  sugar  and  butter  as  for  a 
pie  crust  and  pat  into  9"xl8n  jelly  roll 
pan.  Bake  at  35  0°  until  very  light  brown, 
about  15  minutes.  Let  cool  slightly,  then 
cover  with  custard  made  from  sugar,  baking 
powder,  flour,  eggs,  lemon  juice  and  rind. 
Bake  for  15  or  20  minutes  more,  until  set. 
Cool.  Cut  into  squares  and  sprinkle  with 
powdered  sugar  if  desired.

Madeleines 


3  large  eggs 
2/3  cup  sugar 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

V%    cups  sifted  cake  flour 

5g  teaspoon  double  action  baking  powder 

^  teaspoon  salt 

2  teaspoons  grated  lemon  peel 
3/4  cup  butter,  melted 
Confectioners  sugar 

Beat  eggs  till  lemon  colored  and  4  times 
original  volume.  Beat  in  sugar  and  vanilla. 
Gradually  fold  in  dry  ingredients  and  lemon 
peel.  Stir  in  the  cool  melted  butter.  Spoon 
about  1  Tablespoon  of  batter  into  each  but- 
tered shell,  about  2/3  full.  Bake  in  pre- 
heated oven,  350°  for  12  minutes,  until 
toothpick  comes  out  clean.  Remove  cookies 
to  cooling  rack.  Dust  tops  with  sifted  con- 
fectioners sugar.

2  cups  sugar 
2  cups  water 
Orange  or  lemon  peel 

Chop  or  grind  the  almonds.  Clarify  the  but- 
ter. Take  a  small  pan  that  will  fit  the 
Phyllo  when  cut  in  half.  Place  one  sheet 
of  Phyllo  in  the  buttered  pan  and  brush 
with  butter.  Repeat  this  6  times,  leaving 
the  last  sheet  unbuttered.  Sprinkle  with 
almonds,  evenly.  Place  on  top  of  this 
another  pastry  sheet  and  brush  with  butter, 
then  place  another  sheet  but  do  not  butter. 
Sprinkle  this  sheet  with  almonds,  evenly. 
Repeat  this  procedure  until  you  have  6  or 
7  sheets  left.  Place  these  sheets  on  top 
of  each  other  making  sure  to  brush  each 
one  with  butter.  On  the  last  sheet,  apply 
the  butter  heavily.  Cool.  With  a  sharp  knife 
cut  diamond  shape  pieces,  cutting  all  the  way 
down  to  the  pan.  Bake  at  300°  for  about  lh 
hours,  watching  that  it  does  not  become  too 
dark.  Remove  from  oven  when  a  light  golden 
brown.  Cool.  To  make  the  syrup,  boil  the 
honey,  sugar,  water,  cinnamon  and  peel  until 
it  sheets  from  a  spoon.  Syrup  must  be  quite 
thick  or  the  crisp  pastry  will  become  soggy. 
The  Baclava  must  be  cold  and  the  syrup  boil- 
ing hot  or  vice-versa. 

Penny  Lagakos 


242 


Baclava  -  Syrup 

1  cup  pure  honey 

2  cups  sugar 
2  cups  water 

2  cinnamon  sticks 

A  few  orange  or  lemon  peels 

Boil  until  last  drops  on  spoon  drops  holding 
onto  a  rather  thick  connection  with  the  other 
drop.  Syrup  mus  t  be  quite  thick  or  else  the 
beautifully  crisp  pastry  will  become  soggy. 
The  Baclava  must  be  cold  and  the  syrup  boil- 
ing hot  or  vice-versa.  Let  cool  well  before 
serving.  I  like  to  leave  it  at  least  overnight. 
Do  not  cover  unless  some  is  left  over .  It  keeps 
very  well  outside  or  inside  refrigerator. 


Blond  Brownies 

1/3  cup  shortening 

1  cup  brown  sugar 

1  egg 

1  teaspoon  vanilla 

1  cup  sifted  flour 

h    teaspoon  soda 

h    teaspoon  salt 

1  cup  chocolate  bits  (6  oz  .  ) 

Cream,  shortening  and  sugar.  Add  the  eggs  and 
vanilla  and  beat  well.  Sift  together  the 
flour,  soda  and  salt.  Add  to  the  creamed 
mixture  and  mix  well.  Stir  in  the  chocolate 
bits.  Spread  in  greased  pan,  llVx7^"xl^"  . 
Bake  in  350°  oven  20-25  minutes.  Cut  while 
warm.  Makes  two  dozen  squares. 

Wilma  Packard

Yum-Yums 

2  eggs 

1  cup  butter 

lh    cups  brown  sugar 

2h    cups  sifted  flour 

%  teaspoon  salt 

1  teaspoon  soda 

2  Tablespoons  vanilla 

1  cup  (4  oz .  can)  shredded  coconut 
1  cup  (4  oz  .  can)  English  walnuts 
1  cup  (6%  oz . )  dates,  chopped 

Cream  butter  and  sugar  until  light  and 
fluffy.  Add  eggs,  beat  well,  add  sifted 
flour,  salt  and  soda.  Stir  in  remaining 
ingredients  and  mix  thoroughly.  Drop  by 
teaspoonful  onto  ungreased  cookie  sheet. 
Bake  at  375°  for  8  minutes. 

Susan  Pond 

Chinese  Chews 

1  cup  sugar 

3/4  cup  sifted  flour 

1  teaspoon  baking  powder 
\    teaspoon  salt 

2  eggs,  beaten 

1  cup  dates,  chopped 
1  cup  chopped  nuts 
1  teaspoon  vanilla 

Sift  together  sugar,  flour,  baking  powder 
and  salt.  Combine  beaten  eggs,  dates,  nuts 
and  vanilla.  Combine  egg  mixture  with  the 
flour  mixture.  Mix  lightly  but  thoroughly. 
Place  mixture  in  greased  8ffx8"x2M  pan  and 
bake  at  350°  for  40  minutes.  While  hot,  cut 
in  small  squares  and  roll  each  in  powdered 
sugar .  Yield :  48 . 

Ethel  DeVol

Candied  Orange  Pecans 

2  cups  light  brown  sugar 
\    cup  hot  water 

1  Tablespoon  grated  orange  peel 

2  cups  pecan  halves 

Let  sugar  and  water  boil  to  235   on 
candy  thermometer.   Add  orange  peel  and 
stir.   Add  pecans  and  remove  from  fire. 
Stir  constantly  until  mixture  looks 
creamy.   Pour  out  onto  waxed  paper. 
Separate  nuts  quickly  with  2  forks. 
Let  cool,  then  pack  into  air-tight 
containers . 

Lucy  Lombard! 


Chocolate  Truffles 

24  oz.  sweet  chocolate 

12  oz.  bitter  chocolate 

8  oz .  confectioners  sugar 

1  egg  yolk 

Cocoa 

Powdered  chocolate 

Melt  chocolate  in  top  of  double  boiler. 
Add'  egg,  butter  and  sugar.   Mix  thor- 
oughly.  Let  cool.   Make  little  balls 
or  truffles  and  roll  them  in  cocoa  mixed 
with  powdered  chocolate.   (Nestle*  is  best.) 
For  Rum  triffles,  add  3  teaspoons  rum  to 
chocolate  mixture. 

Gertrude  Marchetti

Pulled  Mints 


3  cups  sugar 
1  cup  water 
1  pinch  salt 
Butter ,  size 


of  walnut 


Bring  the  water,  sugar  and  salt  to  a 
boil.   Add  butter.   Continue  boiling 
without  stirring  until  syrup  makes  a 
hard  ball  in  cold  water.   Pour  on 
greased  marble  slab  and  begin  taking 
it  up  as  it  hardens  on  edge.   Pull  when 
cool  enough  to  handle.   Add  a  few  drops 
of  peppermint  and  coloring  if  desired. 
Cut  with  scissors  onto  waxed  paper  and 
turn  until  pieces  do  not  stick.   Pack 
in  a  tight  box. 

Mrs .  Corbin 


Spiced  Pineapple 

1  lb .  4^  oz.  can  pineapple  chunks,  undrained 

h    cup  vinegar 

12  whole  cloves 

h    cup  sugar 

Grated  peel  of  1  lemon 

3  3"  .sticks  cinnamon 

Combine  all  ingredients,  cover  and  refrig- 
erate for  at  least  one  week.

Gingered  Cranberry  Sauce 

4  cups  cranberries 

1  cup  water 
Pinch  of  salt 

2  cups  sugar 

1/3  cup  crystallized  ginger,  chopped  fine 

Boil  berries  in  water  till  they  pop. 
Remove  from  heat.   Add  sugar,  salt 
and  ginger  and  mix  thoroughly.   Chill. 

Helen  McMahon 


Ginger  Marmalade 

1  orange  (navel) 

1  lemon 

1  white  grapefruit 

1  or  2  cups  crystallized  ginger,  chopped  fine 

Cut  fruit  up  finely  and  cover  with  3  times 
the  amount  of  water.   Let  stand  24  hours. 
Boil  10  minutes.   Let  stand  24  hours.   Add 
an  equal  amount  of  sugar.   Boil  until 
amber  color  about  1-3/4  hours  or  until  of 
the  consistency  of  preserves  (222°).   Be- 
fore removing  from  fire  add  1  or  2  cups 
preserved  ginger  cut  into  small  pieces. 
Cook  one  minute.   Pour  into  jars  (sterilized 
jars)  and  cover  with  parafin. 

Laura  Buckham 


248 


Horseradish  Jelly 

2>h    cups  sugar 

^  cup  prepared  horseradish 

kg  cup  vinegar 

%  cup  Certo 

Place  sugar,  horseradish  and  vinegar  in  a 
large  saucepan  and  stir  over  medium  heat 
until  sugar  is  dissolved.  Add  enough  green 
vegetable  coloring  to  give  it  a  distinct 
green  color.  Bring  to  a  boil,  then  add 
Certo,  stirring  constantly  while  it  is 
brought  to  a  full  rolling  boil.  W,hen  it 
reaches  this  stage  remove  from  heat  and 
pour  quickly  into  sterilized  jelly  glasses. 
Pour  melted  parafin  over  the  glasses. 

Eleanor  Shedd 

Pickled  Beets  and  Eggs 

1  pint  or  1  can  of  sliced  beets 

h    cup  brown  sugar 

%    cup  vinegar 

Jg  cup  water 

\    teaspoon  salt 

Small  piece  of  cinnamon 

3  or  4  cloves 

8  hard  cooked  eggs,  unsliced 

Heat  sugar,  vinegar,  water,  salt  and  spices 
together  for  10  minutes.  Cool  and  pour  over 
the  beets  and  eggs.  Allow  to  stand  24  hours

Sweet  Pickled  Beets 

8  cups  small  whole  beets 

8  onions,  sliced 

2  cups  cider  vinegar 

2  cups  water 

2  Tab  l.e  spoons  pickling  spice 

2  cups  dark  brown  sugar 

2  onions,  chopped 

In  a  covered  pan,  boil  the  vinegar, 
spice,  brown  sugar  and  chopped  onions  for 
10  minutes.   Pour  this  hot  mixture  over 
the  beets  and  sliced  onions.   Bring  to  a 
boil  again  and  then  remove  from  fire. 
Cool  well.   Put  in  refrigerator  for  at 
leas  t  36  hours . 

Lucy  Lombardi 

Snap  Bean  Relish 

1  package  frozen  French  green  beans 

1/3  cup  salad  oil 

6  small  onions,  cut  in  fine  rings 

Juice  of  1  lemon 

1  teaspoon  sugar 

h    teaspoon  pepper 

1  teaspoon  salt 

h    teaspoon  pepper 

Cook  beans  4-5  minutes  only  and  add  other 
ingredients.  Mixture  should  marinate  4-6 
hours  and  be  thoroughly  chilled.
